Opening of the US Democratic Party Convention; Conservative Faction Advocates Party Defection; Roosevelt's Re-election Hopes Diminish 43

Philadelphia: The National Democratic Convention will open at noon, beginning with a speech by Committee Chairman and US Postmaster General Farley. The session will extend into the evening, at which time the Governor of Pennsylvania, Earle, will deliver a welcoming address. The delegates will then hear a major speech by Senator Barkley. President Roosevelt is scheduled to arrive here on Saturday or Sunday and will be chosen by popular vote at an open-air rally as the party's presidential candidate. (Reuters, 23rd)

Philadelphia: The Democratic National Convention is scheduled to open here tomorrow, with most delegates already arrived. According to general consensus, President Roosevelt's re-election, which seemed assured a few months ago, now faces changed circumstances. Strenuous efforts are needed to secure all possible votes before there is hope. The "Old Guard" leader Smith's declaration of war on President Roosevelt, criticisms of the New Deal, and the unbalanced budget are all difficulties encountered at the start of President Roosevelt's campaign. It is widely believed that Smith may invite his friends to support the Republican presidential candidate Landon, and the New Left "Union Party," which has nominated Lemke as its presidential candidate, also appears to be defecting from President Roosevelt. People are now asking if there is any way to prevent the hundreds of thousands of votes supporting President Roosevelt from going to Landon. It is said that the Republican presidential candidate Landon is younger than President Roosevelt, and Hamilton, who leads Landon's campaign, is a capable figure from the Midwest, whose influence cannot be compared with those who ran Hoover's campaign in 1923. However, President Roosevelt's personal appeals to the voters still hold considerable power, and supporters of the New Deal argue that if the criticisms are indeed accurate, then under Landon's proposal for each state to handle its own relief efforts, the situation will inevitably worsen. (Reuters, 22nd)

Philadelphia, USA: The Democratic National Convention will convene here tomorrow. Delegates are firmly supporting President Roosevelt and his New Deal, resisting the party defection movement advocated by conservatives like Smith. However, the current division within the party is unprecedented since former President Roosevelt obstructed former President Taft in the Republican Party in 1912. Democratic National Committee Chairman and Postmaster General Farley responded to yesterday's statement by Smith and others, stating that it represents the views of organizations such as the American Liberty League. Other party leaders also claim that opposition to President Roosevelt is a futile effort. Farley began party activities at 10 a.m. this morning, convening a meeting of the National Committee. It is rumored that once President Roosevelt is re-nominated, he will resign as Postmaster General to focus on election campaigning. State delegates are also holding caucus meetings today to prepare for voting. The biggest point of contention regarding the platform is that New Deal leaders want to draft a radical anti-trust declaration based on government policy. There are two main keys: one is to win the support of Senator Borah, who also advocates anti-trust, and the other is to prevent farmers who oppose monopolies from turning to Lemke's United Third Party. During today's National Committee meeting, when former Massachusetts Governor Ely and current Georgia Governor Talmadge were called upon, they remained silent, making people deeply feel that opponents of the New Deal are indeed likely to defect. However, Talmadge subsequently stated that he does not intend to leave the Democratic Party, as all issues should be resolved within the party. (National Press, 22nd)

Philadelphia, USA: Political observers familiar with the situation here believe today that the developments of the past two days have forced the Democratic Party to lean to the left. It is said that if President Roosevelt wants to be re-nominated, his platform must surpass that of United Third Party candidate Lemke. The Democratic National Convention's strategy should be to win over Western states by having Senators La Follette, Sheppard, Norris, and others support the New Deal. La Follette is a Progressive, Sheppard is a Labor-Farmer, and Norris is a Progressive Republican. All of them supported Roosevelt in 1932. Today, Roosevelt's camp has gained a glimmer of hope with the support of New York Governor Lehman. Lehman is a close friend of both President Roosevelt and Smith, who has declared his intention to defect. He recently declared that he does not wish to be governor again, and some quarters believe that President Roosevelt will lose a good supporter. Now that he has declared his support, it shows that he is still loyal to the New Deal. (National Press, 22nd)

Chien Tang River's Water Level Suddenly Rises; Dyke Construction Along the River is Quite Dangerous; Chien Tang River Bridge is Also Affected 68

Hangchow Correspondence: Because of the recent continuous rain and mold in counties of the upper reaches of Chien Tang River, mountain floods are erupting, with water flowing downwards with extraordinary impetuosity. The water level of the Chien Tang River is usually only about six meters and forty-five centimeters, but at 7 p.m. on the 22nd, it suddenly rose sharply to eight meters and four centimeters and five centimeters, only a few centimeters below the highest water level of last year. Dyke construction along the river is quite dangerous. The Water Conservancy Engineering Office of the Construction Department has specially ordered the engineering team to pay special attention to protection at all times. The Chien Tang River Bridge project was considerably affected by the great flood last year. On the 22nd, when the fifth caisson of the bridge was under construction, it was suddenly hit by huge waves. The caisson, together with its iron anchor weighing about 800 tons, was swept several miles downstream to Nanshingchiao. The Bridge Construction Office dispatched a small steamer to tow it, but due to the high tide and rapid water, it was almost capsized, and construction had to be stopped. The eleventh caisson on the north bank was also washed away and moved, making construction impossible. As for the pile-driving project, seven of the eight bridge piers have been completed, and only one pier remains. However, all projects must be considerably affected. Fortunately, the water level had dropped several centimeters to eight meters and twenty-five centimeters on the morning of the 23rd, but there is still a tendency to continue to rise when the tide comes in the evening.

East of the 104th breakwater dam on the south bank of the Chien Tang River, the river bank is in danger of collapsing due to repeated attacks by the Chien Tang River tide. The Siaoshan County Government and local people have earnestly requested the Construction Department to find a way to provide relief. After receiving the report, the Construction Department plans to send a team in early next month to measure the shape of the riverbed and riverbank near the east of Hsihsing Wharf, so as to carry out the protection plan. The required survey fee has been approved and allocated. (23rd)

City of Nanking Conducting Land Registration in Rural Areas; Implementing Land Tax Collection and Compiling Land Register Maps, etc. 69

Nanking Correspondence: Land registration in the city districts of Nanking is scheduled to be completed in the 34th year of the Republic. The land in the remaining suburban rural areas, after the provincial and municipal boundaries are drawn, should belong to the municipal area. It covers an area of more than 600,000 mu, accounting for more than 8.5% of the city's area. It is divided into four districts: Yentzuchiao, Shanghsinho, Hsialingwei, and the mausoleum park, most of which is farmland, collectively called the municipal rural area. Previously, although the land in these areas had been reported by Kiangning County, the boundaries had not been clearly demarcated and the land register had not been corrected. In order to complete the consolidation of land throughout the city, the Nanking Municipal Land Administration Bureau plans to continue to conduct land registration in rural areas starting in fiscal year 25. However, since the situation in urban and rural areas is quite different, the procedures must be simplified to avoid protracted delays. It has drafted an outline for handling land registration in rural areas, submitted it for approval and implementation, and is now preparing to conduct triangulation and topographic surveys in each rural area starting in July of this year, and then issue announcements to notify the households in each rural area to conduct surveys on a regular basis. At the same time, prepare a general registration map and begin registration, starting with Shanghsinho and progressing according to the decision, with the aim of completing it within two years.

The Nanking Municipal Government plans to implement the collection of land value tax and land appreciation tax in the registered areas starting in fiscal year 25, with the aim of realizing our party's land policy, equally distributing the burden on citizens, and enriching the funds for municipal construction. It is now engaged in various preparatory tasks. The estimate of land prices will still be handled by the Municipal Government Valuation Committee. Other matters, such as the distinction between tax lands and the setting of tax rates, are also being discussed separately. This plan can be realized in the 25th year of the Republic.

Other matters, such as the planning of land use, the implementation of geological exploration, the clearing of public land, and the compilation of land register maps, are all planned to be held in the shortest possible time.

Intensified Air Defense Training for the Public in Various Counties of Guangdong Province; Seventy Percent of Air Defense Associations Established, with Rapid Preparation of Branches in Districts and Townships 70

Guangzhou Dispatch: The Guangdong provincial authorities, recognizing the escalating urgency of the global situation and the critical importance of air defense equipment, have recently launched an active plan to strengthen the province's overall air defense capabilities, educate the public on air defense knowledge, and practice air defense methods. The implementation steps involve instructing the pacification commissioners in each district to establish air defense committees responsible for all related matters. It has been observed that since their establishment, these committees have been actively training the public in rescue, disinfection, shelter procedures, and the development of transportation, all crucial aspects of air defense work. Cities and towns within these districts have also been actively establishing air defense associations to assist in these efforts. Currently, seventy percent of the counties and cities in the province have established air defense associations, and the remaining counties, cities, districts, and townships are rapidly preparing to establish branch associations, aiming to complete the provincial air defense plan in the near future.

Guangdong Imposes a Special Tax on Imported Timber; Ten Percent of the Value Extracted in Addition to Customs Duties, with Discretionary Exemption for Industry-Related Materials 71

Guangzhou Dispatch: Starting from the 15th of this month, Guangdong Province has begun collecting a special tax on imported timber. The special tax bureau for imported agricultural products will levy ten percent of the value reported on the customs declaration. It is estimated that this tax will increase monthly revenue by more than 60,000 yuan. The categories of taxable timber are listed below: Timber products include planks, ordinary squared timber (excluding teak and listed timbers), logs, heavy timber, light timber, ordinary sawn timber (including those that are not merely sawn, but not including masts), heavy timber (a) without defects in weight, (b) clean weight suitable for commercial use; light timber, ordinary masts, railway sleepers, teak (beam and plank sections), unlisted timbers, persimmon wood, agarwood, fragrant incense, rosewood, padauk, sandalwood, *Dalbergia tonkinensis*, lignum vitae, fragrant wood, aromatic wood (fragrant firewood), cork, stopper wood, and others (including camphorwood, ebony, *Vitex parviflora*, ironwood, etc.). Japanese wood shavings, decorative wood, various wooden wares and unlisted products including (a) barrels, boxes, cages, and other ordinary packing containers, (b) cork stoppers, (c) furniture, (d) machinery (parts or components), (e) wood chips (for match production), (f) barrel and box staves, (g) matchsticks (for match production), (h) and other types. It is also noted that "heavy timber" refers to timber from coniferous and thorn-leaved trees that produce cones. The imposition of this special tax on imported timber will significantly impact local handicrafts. Industries related to imported timber are actively petitioning for the exclusion of essential items from the tax. Specifically, the newly taxed wood chips and matchsticks are raw materials for the local match industry. As there is a shortage of wood chips and matchsticks domestically, the imposition of this special tax will inevitably affect the match industry. Following requests from match merchants, the Finance Department has approved the exclusion of wood chips and matchsticks from the special tax. Recently, sandalwood merchants petitioned the Finance Department to exempt sandalwood, agarwood, fragrant incense, and fragrant firewood from the special tax, citing the precedent of wood chips and matchsticks to support local industry. Their reasoning is that these timbers are primarily used as raw materials for locally made incense. There is no domestic production of these timbers, which not only contributes to industry but also benefits agriculture. Furthermore, these fragrant woods are already subject to customs duties upon import, with taxes ranging from four cents per hundred catties to twenty-five percent of the value, creating a heavy burden. The merchants fear that with the addition of a special tax, many stores will struggle to survive. After reviewing the petition, the Finance Department deemed the claims to be factual. It has exempted *Dalbergia tonkinensis* and *Caesalpinia sappan* from the special tax, but they will still be subject to the dye tax. It has been observed that Guangdong Province has a large market for imported timber, and there are significant stocks of old inventory. The Finance Department originally set the deadline for inventory registration as the 14th. However, due to requests from merchants who felt the registration period was too short, the special tax bureau has extended the deadline for inventory registration to the 20th of this month (June 19th).

Smuggling into Jinan Intensifies; Customs and Tax Losses Estimated at Over 1.8 Million 72

Jinan Dispatch: In recent weeks, due to the unstable situation, smuggling in North China has intensified, and the influx of smuggled goods into Jinan has increased. According to reliable sources, from the 11th to the 21st of this month, smuggled goods entering the city include 3,173 bundles of rayon, 406 cases of cigarette paper, 215 pieces of cloth, 12 items of material, and 710 tons, plus 703 items, of white sugar. Assuming each bundle of rayon is valued at 170 yuan, the total value is 639,410 yuan. Each case of cigarette paper is valued at 160 yuan, for a total value of 64,960 yuan. Considering the remaining cloth, materials, and white sugar, the total loss in customs duties and various taxes is estimated to be over 1,868,000 yuan. (June 21st)

Songjiang: Nine-Year-Old Girl Raped 73

Zhang Gao, a resident of Sixing Town, whose husband works in Baoying, has a son and a daughter. The daughter, named A'nan, is nine years old. The night before last, Zhang Gao went to help at a *zongzi* (glutinous rice dumpling) store in the central market, leaving her young daughter at home to watch the door. Wu Xiangsheng, aged twenty-nine, suddenly broke in and raped the young girl. When the mother returned, she heard her daughter crying in pain and found her pants covered in blood. Realizing something was wrong, she questioned her daughter, who explained what had happened. She reported the incident to the local police station, which transferred the case to Songjiang. According to Wu Xiangsheng's confession, he had a previous affair with Zhang Gao and was falsely accused because she refused to give him rice. However, A'nan identified him in court, and he finally admitted his guilt. The Public Security Bureau has transferred the case to the Procuratorate of the local court for further investigation. Wu Xiangsheng has been detained, and Zhang A'nan has been sent to Rongcheng Hospital for examination. Zhang Gao has been sent home.

After the arrest of these vagrants, society has become more peaceful, and the people are greatly pleased.

Dispute Over the Unloading of Stolen Coal 78

Since the illicit coal from Liujiang was transported from Cheng to Wuxi by unscrupulous merchants Zhu Changshou, Ma Echu, and Mi Yuehun, who formed the Hexing Company, it was subsequently seized by the Detective Team of the Public Security Bureau. The stolen coal was impounded and reported to the Commissioner's Office. Later, Mr. Konoe Shinsuke, a Japanese staff member from Mitsui & Co. in Shanghai, came to Wuxi to negotiate. As a result, the Commissioner's Office released the stolen coal. However, the cargo handlers refused to unload it, leaving the stolen coal still loaded on thirteen boats and unable to be unloaded ashore. The boatmen faced starvation, leading to several disputes. On the 22nd, Wang Junshi and Zhu Songtao, Chinese staff members from Mitsui & Co. in Cheng, came to Wuxi and hired more than ten cargo handlers to secretly unload the coal at night, intending to unload the stolen coal into Zhang Wanyuan's liquor store. However, cargo handlers each have their own territory. The unloading operation was discovered by other cargo handlers, who gathered to protest. Wang Junshi refused to stop unloading, and the two sides were taken to the Second Police Precinct. Officers ordered them to resolve the dispute outside the station. However, after leaving the station, the coal owner instructed the boatmen and workers to continue unloading. By around 10:00 PM, only a few dozen tons of the stolen coal (approximately one boatload) had been unloaded. The boat owner then sought settlement for the boat and meal expenses from Jing Heling (an ophthalmologist), the representative of the coal owner, who refused to pay a single cent. Upon hearing this, the other boatmen automatically stopped unloading midway. At the same time, Zhang Deqi, the owner of Zhang Wanyuan's liquor store, upon learning the inside story of the stolen coal, also published a statement declaring that he would not allow the storage of stolen coal. The storage of the stolen coal was a result of the coal owner's coercion. Therefore, the coal incident is still difficult to resolve for the time being.

Changshu: School Principals Request Allocation of Accumulated Debt 79

Since the 19th fiscal year to the 23rd fiscal year, the expenses of the various schools in this county have suffered from financial constraints. The Education Bureau has been unable to release funds on a monthly basis, resulting in accumulated debts of more than ten installments over the past four years. Subsequently, after the implementation of the treasury system in the 23rd fiscal year, these expenses were listed under accumulated debt. Some deceased and retired teachers were paid a small amount. As there is no clear timeframe for repayment, and as this year's new and old grain tax collection is at its peak, and educational funds are also relatively abundant, more than ten principals from Taqian, Xueqian, Yangang, and other schools have jointly petitioned the bureau, requesting that the accumulated debt be allocated in regular installments in accordance with the prescribed standard to provide some compensation.

Yesterday was the Dragon Boat Festival, which is traditionally the first major settlement period of the year for businesses. The reasons for this success are that merchants have been more cautious about extending credit in recent years, ensuring that accounts are reliable and stable, and the collection rate is better. Furthermore, banks have been more active in lending this year, helping businesses with their financial turnover, and operations in various sectors have shown some improvement. As a result, industries such as silk fabrics, foreign goods, and mountain products have seen profits.

Zhenjiang: Tea Worker Rapes Young Girl 83

Du Shuyi, a painter, brought his family to Zhenjiang in early this month and stayed at Room 28 of the Yangzi Hotel on Yingjiang Road, planning to exhibit his works. They examined her and found bloodstains on her undergarments. Suspecting something was wrong, they gathered all the servants and asked the girl to identify the perpetrator. The girl pointed to Chen Changhua as the culprit. They immediately called the police, who arrested Chen and took him to the local police station, which then transferred him to the court. After the prosecutor opened the court for questioning, Du Shuyi recounted the above incident and presented the bloodstained pants as evidence. The defendant, Chen Changhua, vehemently denied the accusation. An examination was then conducted, and the forensic doctor determined that the girl's hymen had been ruptured. However, due to incomplete surgical instruments, it was difficult to determine whether the injury was caused by trauma or by the genitals. Ningbo: Mother and Four Children Commit Suicide by Drowning 88

Zheng Caifang, a resident of Caotou Xianggongfang in the 7th District of Zhenhai, is a pastry maker. His wife, Liu, has two sons and a daughter: Shenyao, 6 years old; Shenxiang, 2 years old; and Shen'e, 4 years old. Zheng Caifang's Xinshinan goods store, which he opened in Chaiqiao, failed two years ago. Last year, he went to Shanghai to do business on the recommendation of friends and relatives, but again lost his job and returned home. His younger brother, Jifang, a craftsman, believed that with a family of five bringing in no income, it was not beneficial to him. Therefore, on the 5th day of last month, he gathered relatives and friends to separate the households. A few days ago, in order to pay the association fee of eight jiao in silver, he pledged the tin table and the association certificate. As a result, Zheng Caifang and Liu became increasingly negative and often contemplated suicide. On the evening of the 20th, the family had no food for the next day and had only watery rice for dinner. Zheng Caifang, seeing this, went out with tears in his eyes to watch a show at the Chaishimiao temple. Liu, fearing that something might happen, asked her father-in-law to find him. Her father-in-law refused. Liu felt that her situation was precarious and the future with her husband was bleak, so she resolved to commit suicide. At around 8:00 PM that evening, she tied her two sons and one daughter together, carried them to the Zhengjia shore of the Houcao stream, and jumped into the water. They all drowned. When Zheng Caifang returned home and saw the door wide open and no one answered his calls, he rushed to the riverbank and saw his wife and four children floating lifeless in the water. He cried out for help, and when they were pulled ashore, it was too late to save them. Zheng Caifang, in his grief, also wanted to throw himself into the water, but he was prevented from doing so by several of his cousins, who took care of him. The incident was reported to the township office, and coffins were prepared for the burial. Those who heard of it were filled with sorrow.

Sir Leith-Ross Departs Shanghai Yesterday; Sung Tzu-wen, British Chargé d'Affaires, and Others Give Warm Farewell; Hall-Patch and Rogers Appointed to Continue Staying in China 90

Sir Frederick Leith-Ross, the British Commissioner specially sent to China to investigate economic conditions and the chief advisor to the British Treasury, along with his wife and female secretary, Miss Crakner, departed Shanghai yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM aboard the British Company's *Rawalpindi*. Sung Tzu-wen, standing committee member of the National Economic Council and chairman of the Bank of China, personally accompanied his wife, along with the British Chargé d'Affaires to China, Mr. Howe, and his wife, who came specially from Tianjin to give a warm farewell. Details are as follows:

Departure from Shanghai Amidst Firecrackers

The ship was docked at the Eleventh and Twelfth buoys on the river. On the Chinese side, the Jianghai Customs' *Jinghui* small steamer was specially prepared for Sir Leith-Ross to board, along with a large number of firecrackers to celebrate his departure. At 2:10 PM, he departed from the Cathay Hotel to the new Customs wharf. After shaking hands and exchanging pleasantries with the farewell party, he boarded the ship amidst the sound of firecrackers. Mr. and Mrs. Sung accompanied him directly to the *Rawalpindi* before returning. The ship then weighed anchor and departed Shanghai at 4:00 PM sharp.

Warm Farewell from Various Chinese and British Representatives

Those who went to the ship to bid farewell included, in addition to Mr. and Mrs. Sung and the British Chargé d'Affaires and his wife, Mr. Chen Xing, Vice President of the Central Bank, representing Mr. Kong Hsiang-hsi, the Deputy Premier of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance; Secretary Chen Bingzhang; Mr. Zheng Lai, Director of the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance; Mr. Younge, British Advisor to the Ministry of Finance; Sir Brenan, the British Consul General in Shanghai; Mr. Bell, Commercial Counselor; Mr. George, Air Attaché; Mr. Barkham, Chinese Language Counselor of the British Embassy; Secretary Grahame; British Consul Mr. Lamb; and over thirty individuals from the Chinese banking community, including Sung Han-chang, Hsu Hsin-liu, Li Fu-sun, Hu Pi-chiang, Sung Tzu-liang, Pei Sung-sun, Hsi Teh-mou, Sung Tzu-an, etc. Minister Kong, Mr. and Mrs. Sung, and the British Consul General and his wife also presented many flower baskets to Mr. and Mrs. Leith-Ross to wish them a good journey.

Two Assistants Continue to Stay in China

Mr. E. Hall-Patch and Mr. C. Rogers, the assistants to Leith-Ross, only went to the ship to bid farewell and did not travel with him. Hall-Patch has been appointed as the financial advisor to the British embassies in both China and Japan. Rogers has been appointed to remain in China to continue unfinished work. Hall-Patch was originally a senior official in the British Treasury, and Rogers is a senior officer at a London bank.

Expected to Arrive in England in Late Next Month

Sir Leith-Ross is returning directly to London to report on his mission. He will not be staying in any cities along the way. According to the ship's itinerary, he is expected to arrive in England in late next month. His written report has already been sent to England in advance. Sir Leith-Ross arrived in Shanghai on September 21 of last year, making his stay a total of nine months and two days.

Reporters from *L'Impartial* interviewed responsible members of the financial community yesterday morning. They expressed the following opinions regarding Leith-Ross's statements: Leith-Ross's statements can be roughly divided into four parts. The first part describes the silver crisis that China has encountered since 1934 and the measures taken by the Chinese financial authorities to deal with this crisis and their effectiveness. The second part states that although China has tried its best to avoid the silver crisis, its economic situation has not yet reached its best due to the lack of a solid financial system, the unrest in inland security, and the unresolved special problems of North China. The third part calls for a reduction in tariffs. The fourth part mentions that British investment in China has extremely profound opinions, in other words, expresses real guarantees. It only needs to read his speech about the fact that Britain has expressed a lot of sympathy for China, but in this gift in the state of deterioration of Sino-Japanese relations, this problem cannot be denied. Therefore, if we want to achieve the stability and progress of China's economy, we must first adjust the international situation. The United Kingdom, the United States and other countries have invested heavily in China and have a deep relationship with the economy of the Far East. I sincerely hope that they can take the position of morality and justice to create a stable international relationship, so that China can realize its economic construction and the national economy can gradually become prosperous. At that time, it will be more difficult to develop import and export trade than to reduce tax rates. Sir Leith-Ross’s conclusion is nothing more than wanting China to import some key goods. If we speak with an open and fair attitude, China is very willing to become a large market for various countries, but the reason for the degradation of international quality trade for many years lies in the aggression of improper political and military forces from abroad and the improper disasters outside the country and rural areas. Bankruptcy, if the United Kingdom and the United States can develop China's heavy industry and agriculture with a large amount of capital from a friendly standpoint, the vast majority of Chinese laborers can increase their purchasing power, which is actually beneficial to all countries. In short, under the current situation in China, its economic aspect has a relationship with Britain and the United States. China's prosperity and decline will affect Europe and the United States, so I sincerely hope that all countries will provide effective assistance to China, so that the development of China's economy will also help its domestic trade increase and move towards a situation of co-existence and co-prosperity.

Yesterday was the forty-second birthday of the British Emperor Edward VIII. The British troops stationed in Shanghai held a parade at the racecourse. Ministry of Finance Announces the Establishment of Five Provincial Tax Bureaus; The Original Agencies Will Be Merged and Reorganized Separately; Jing Yan and Others Will Be Directors of the Three District Bureaus 95

According to Shenshi News Agency, in order to adjust the tax organization in the five provinces of Hunan, Jiangxi, Hubei, Henan and Sichuan, the Ministry of Finance submitted to the central government for approval to establish the Hubei-Henan, Hunan-Jiangxi, and Sichuan Three District Tax Bureaus. The official announcement was made yesterday by ministerial order. The original text stated, "The various unified taxes, tobacco and alcohol taxes, and mineral product taxes under the jurisdiction of the Tax Department of the Ministry have always been set up as separate agencies to collect taxes separately. The organization is very fragmented, and the command is not unified, which makes inspection difficult and easily breeds malpractices. After repeated and thorough rectification, although some effects have been achieved, there is still a lack of significant results. The crux of the problem lies in this. Unless a fundamental reform is carried out, it will be difficult to achieve a thorough reorganization. In view of this, the Ministry has drafted an outline for unifying the tax agencies in various provinces and reforming the tobacco and alcohol tax methods, which was submitted to the 262nd meeting of the Executive Yuan for deliberation and approval. It should be implemented in accordance with the order. The Ministry has now decided to implement it in the five provinces of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, Henan, and Sichuan, starting from the 25th year, and has designated Hunan and Jiangxi as one district, Hubei and Henan as one district, and Sichuan as two districts. In addition to the original Henan Province under the jurisdiction of the Luyu District General Tax Bureau, which has now been transferred to the jurisdiction of Hubei and Henan, the Unified Tax Bureau should be changed to the East District General Tax Bureau. The various unified taxes, tobacco and alcohol taxes agencies within the five provinces of Hunan, Jiangxi, Hubei, Henan, and Sichuan under the jurisdiction of each district shall be separately reduced, merged, and reorganized. Each district shall establish a district tax bureau to specifically supervise the collection of matters, and consider the situation and delineate areas in the five provinces to establish sub-district tax management offices and tax sub-offices to specialize in tax collection affairs. In addition to the temporary regulations separately formulated by the Ministry for promulgation and implementation, and reported to the Executive Yuan for special filing and separate announcements, it is hereby announced. This order."

It is also learned that the candidates for the directors of the three district tax bureaus have also been announced by the Ministry of Finance by ministerial order. Jing Youyan will act as the director of the Hubei-Henan District Tax Bureau, Ding Chungao will act as the director of the Hunan-Jiangxi District Tax Bureau, Zai Zongzhu will act as the director of the Sichuan District Tax Bureau, and Qu Dacheng and other twenty-one people will be the directors of the twenty-one sub-district tax management offices such as Hankou.

German Goods Imported to Shanghai Increased Sharply in May, Thirteen Times More Than the Same Period Last Year 96

According to Shenshi News Agency, Germany's trade with China has always been dominated by heavy industry. In recent years, German goods imported to China have suddenly increased. In mid-April this year, German goods imported to Shanghai accounted for the first place in Shanghai's imports. The total amount imported in May was 12,737,716 yuan, a sharp decrease of 2,515,887 yuan compared to the 10,221,829 yuan in April, an increase of 25%. Compared with the statistics of German goods imported in May last year, which was 5,424,658 yuan, it has soared by 135%. The rate of increase is really amazing. Some commentators believe that this is due to the difference in the conversion of customs gold units into silver dollars. In May last year, the average was 1 customs gold unit equals 1.63 yuan of national currency, while this year the average customs gold unit has risen to 2.262 yuan. Therefore, the reporter specially inquired from the customs to obtain the figures in gold unit for publication as follows: May was 5,653,669 customs gold units, and April was 4,518,934 customs gold units, an increase of 25%. Compared with the 3,319,864 customs gold units in May last year, the increase of 2,338,05 customs gold is still a sharp increase of more than 70%. Among the German goods imported to Shanghai in May, the highest increase rate was wheat. The import in April was only 2,407 customs gold units, and in May it was 411,677 customs gold units, a sharp increase of more than 40 customs gold. Other items such as metals and ores have also increased significantly, and the proportion of machinery, tools, and dyes has also increased by more than one time, setting a new record in recent years.

Overseas Chinese Urgently Hope That the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Will Open a China-Malaysia Shipping Route 97

According to the Dagong News Agency, the International Trade Bureau reported the recent situation of the China-Malaysia shipping route by the Consulate in Penang, saying that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company recently borrowed money from the Boxer Indemnity Committee and Shanghai banking circles to build new ships to run between China and Malaysia. The China-Malaysia shipping route has always been manipulated by foreign ships, and Chinese ships have occupied a very small position, which is even worse in recent years. In the past, Qiu Changbo, a former wealthy man in this island, built many large ships such as Zhangzhou, Fujian, and Haicheng, which sailed to Penang, Singapore, Hong Kong, Shantou, and Xiamen, etc. This was the beginning of Chinese merchants opening up the China-Malaysia shipping route. Later, there were Lin Zhenzong, a giant merchant in Yangon, and Lin Heban, a giant merchant in Singapore. Lin Zhenzong had many large ships such as Shuangchun, Shuang'an, and Shuangguo, each with a load of 7,000 to 8,000 tons or 10,000 tons. Hufeng Company had Fengqing, Fengping, and Fengsheng, which has been discontinued, Fenghua, Fengmao, Fengyuan, which sank in Shantou port, and Fengxiang, which is now sailing, and many other ships, all with a load of 4,000 to 5,000 tons or 6,000 to 7,000 tons, all running between China, Malaysia, and Yangon. However, times have changed, and the situation is different from the past. Qiu Changbo, the founder of the China-Malaysia shipping route opened up by Chinese merchants, after his death, the large ships he operated, such as Fujian, Zhangzhou, and Haicheng, are no longer seen. Lin Zhenzong, who continued to open up the China-South shipping route, and his large ships such as Shuangmei, Shuang'an, and Shuangguo, have also been sold to foreigners for operation due to the environment. Now, the only Chinese ship left is Hufeng. Hufeng was originally entirely Chinese capital. In 1932, it cooperated with the British company Delee Steamship Company and changed to a limited company, thus becoming a Sino-British joint venture. The Chinese ships sailing between China and Malaysia have gone from prosperity to decline. As a result, foreign ships are rampant and almost entirely occupied by foreign ships. Suddenly, our China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has a proposal to open the China-Malaysia shipping route. Overseas Chinese are all overjoyed. If this proposal can be realized, it can slightly recover the rights and interests and make up for the loopholes.

The Ant Troupe's Third Performance Was Banned Again Yesterday Morning; The Three Plays Were All Approved by the Education Bureau; More Than a Thousand Spectators Were Frustrated and Helpless 102

According to Huadong News Agency, following the Experimental Troupe of Xingqi, the third performance of the Ant Troupe, which was scheduled to be held at the Hushe Theater on Beijing Road yesterday morning, was banned by the Public Works Department again. The purpose of this performance by the troupe is to: 1. Contact troupe members for Dragon Boat Festival entertainment; 2. Sell tickets to provide for troupe expenses. The three plays performed, "Smuggling," "Poison," and "Bugle," were all approved by the Education Bureau. This sudden ban has caused more than a thousand spectators to be frustrated and helpless, as they were not aware of the details beforehand and most went to the meeting before 9:00 to watch. Several hundred spectators even burst into tears because of this.

Repeatedly Changed the Repertoire The troupe is affiliated with the Ant Society and aims to connect troupe members' feelings. All previous performances were free tickets and invitations to troupe members, relatives, and friends. The first time there were more than 200 spectators, and the second time there were more than 600 spectators. This time was the third performance. In order to raise troupe expenses, tickets were sold at a price of 50 cents by the Commercial Press. More than a thousand tickets have been sold so far. The original program was "Smuggling," "Bugle," and "Who Killed the Baby," all of which were approved by the Municipal Education Bureau. Later, because the play "Who Killed the Baby" was inconvenient for today's Children's Year, the play "Poison" was temporarily changed.

Finally Banned by the Concession The troupe went through several preparations and changed the program several times, and finally decided to perform at the Hushe Theater yesterday morning. The morning was to entertain troupe members, but suddenly there was an obstacle and it was finally stopped. The reason was the ban by the Public Works Department. The announcement is recorded as follows: "Our troupe was originally scheduled to hold the third performance today, performing the three plays "Smuggling," "Poison," and "Bugle." We suddenly received a notice from the Hushe Theater that the Public Works Department ordered the venue to be stopped and must be rescheduled. The date and location will be announced again. The matter is in a hurry. Thank you for your journey. Please be aware of it."

Iron Ministry Responds to Banking Association: Freight Receipts Not Allowed for Discounting; Three Restrictions on Longhai Consignment Notes; Planned Implementation in Stages 108

The Shanghai Banking Association previously sent a letter to the Ministry of Railways requesting that freight receipts be made negotiable, treated as consignment notes, and inquiring about the three restrictions on consignment notes issued by the Longhai Railway. The Ministry of Railways has now responded to the Banking Association, explaining why freight receipts cannot be approved for discounting to prevent abuses. The details are as follows:

Longhai Railway's Report: The Longhai Railway Engineering and Transportation Departments jointly submitted a report to the Ministry of Railways stating that due to incomplete facilities at various stations along the line, consignment notes are initially only issued at eight stations, including Dapu, which have warehouses. Other stations lack warehouses and cargo sheds, making it extremely difficult to safeguard goods and preventing simultaneous implementation. However, to promote broader adoption, warehouses are being selectively constructed. This year, Weinan, Xi'an, and Lianyungang stations have been added to the list of stations issuing consignment notes. Currently, the first phase of construction is planned for warehouses at twelve stations: Huangkou, Dangshan, Mamuji, Liuhe, Minquan, Lanfeng, Kaifeng, Zhongmu, Sishui, Luodong, Shanzhou, and Lingbao. The second phase will include twenty-two stations: A’huzhen, Xin’anzhen, Wayao, PaoChe, Yunhe, BaChaji, Xuzhou, Lizhuang, Yangji, Heishiguan, Yanshi County, Zhangjingpu, Shengchi, Guanyintang, Changjiawan, Pantouzhen, Wendizhen, Qilicun, Huazhou, Chishui, Lingkou, and Xinfengzhen. The remaining stations are planned for the third phase. Consignment notes will be issued as soon as the warehouses are completed. Regarding waterway-railway combined transport consignment notes, agreement has been reached with the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. Regarding the printing format, a sample has been drafted based on the Ministry's regulations and sent to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company for approval. Follow-up reminders have been sent, and a fixed date for implementation will be set upon receiving their response. Ministry regulations stipulate that consignment notes are only issued at the request of the shipper, and the request must be noted in the special instructions column of the shipping order. To ensure that shippers understand and utilize this system, widespread publicity will be conducted.

Ministry of Railways' Reply: After receiving the report, the Ministry of Railways responded to the Banking Association, stating that "Your Association's official letter of May 12th is acknowledged. The regulations for the use of consignment notes and freight receipts are different. Consignment notes can be freely discounted and transferred with strict procedures. Freight receipts do not have such procedures, and it is not appropriate to allow them to be discounted to prevent abuses. Regarding the three restrictions on the issuance of consignment notes by the Longhai Railway, as reported by the railway, a phased implementation plan is in progress. We have sent the original report for your reference."

Eurasia Company Builds New Hangar: Cost Approximately 140,000 Yuan; Completion in Two Weeks 109

The new hangar being built by Eurasia Aviation Corporation at Longhua Airport is nearing completion. The building is over 200 feet wide and 150 feet deep, facing south. The center is an aircraft hangar 165 feet wide and 110 feet deep, capable of accommodating four of the largest three-engine airliners. Eight iron gates open and close using a sliding mechanism. On the left and right are two-story buildings 20 feet wide. The front sections are semicircular and protrude on both sides of the main entrance, while the rear sections are single-story factory buildings. The entire building is constructed of purple Taishan facing bricks and cement, with harmonious colors. Regarding the use of the buildings, the rear and east-side ground floors are workshops, including metalworking, electric welding, blacksmithing, steel refining, painting, and carpentry shops. The upper floor of the east side is a radio room. The front of the west side houses offices on both floors, while the rear houses a passenger lounge on the ground floor and a storage area above. The roof is a flat platform, with large doors on the east and west sides for staff and passenger access. Completion is expected in two weeks. The company is said to be planning a dedication ceremony, inviting guests from all sectors to visit. The building design was drafted by Xi Fuquan and constructed by Shen Shengji & Co., at a cost of approximately 140,000 yuan.

Details of Commodity Inspection Bureau's Silk Industry Representatives Meeting 111

The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry convened a meeting of silk industry representatives from Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Sichuan, and Shandong at the International Trade Bureau conference room on the afternoon of the 22nd. Attendees included Tan Xihong, Cai Wuji, Xia Daoxiang, Miao Zhongxiu, He Shangping, Dr. Mary, and silk industry representatives such as Zhu Jing'an, Shen Huachen, Huang Jiwen, Xu Ligeng, Xu Shouyi, Xue Zukang, Huang Bingruo, Zheng Haiquan, Hu Zhongming, Zhang Xinyuan, Hu Weigai, and Zhang Zhuping, Yin Buting, and more than twenty others. Chairman Cai Wuji began by reporting the purpose of the meeting, stating that the bureau had been ordered by the Ministry in March to prepare for raw silk quality inspection. Progress over the past few months had been smooth, but the matter was significant and related to the future of China's silk industry. Therefore, representatives were invited to the bureau to discuss the matter jointly, gather opinions, and learn from each other. Then, Miao Zhongxiu reported on the progress of the preparations, stating that the Japanese government had implemented mandatory raw silk quality inspection long ago. To learn from neighboring countries' implementation methods, he was sent to Japan to study raw silk inspection policies. After returning, he ordered various new-style inspection machines and instruments from home and abroad, recruited and trained technical personnel, and expanded the original location to actively prepare for the inspection. A preliminary raw silk grade table was drafted and distributed to silk merchants for reference. The original plan was to start implementation on July 1st, but because the installation of machinery takes a long time, it is proposed to submit to the Ministry to change the official implementation date to August 1st. Afterwards, Director Tan Xihong gave his opinion on raw silk inspection, stating that the methods and standards of raw silk quality inspection must be discussed by silk merchants to ensure that both buyers and sellers benefit. Now that industries are trending towards standardization and science, raw silk inspection has reached the point of standard implementation, but the power rests with the buyer, and disputes are inevitable. To prepare proper methods, the government will preside over the inspection, ensuring fair inspection between buyers and producers. The establishment of grades should be based on existing precedents of production, consumption, and competition, with the hope of preparing for grade inspection within one year. Silk industry representatives Zhu Jing'an and Shen Huachen expressed their support for the government's raw silk inspection policy and hoped for cooperation between the government and businesses. Finally, it was decided to implement raw silk quality inspection on August 1st of this year, and to implement raw silk grade inspection after the new silk appears next year. During this one-year preparation period, proper methods should be researched to ensure timely implementation. This decision will be submitted to the Ministry of Industry for approval before implementation.

Zhejiang General Chamber of Commerce Requests Suspension of Special Construction Tax 112

Letter Sent to Zhejiang Donation and Tax Supervision Committee: Stop Extension Upon Expiration

The Zhejiang General Chamber of Commerce, located at Lianzhu Lane, Avenue Edward VII, sent a letter to the Zhejiang Provincial Donation and Tax Supervision Committee yesterday, stating that the burden of taxes in Zhejiang is heaviest in western Zhejiang, and the largest additional tax on land is the special construction tax. The total amount of silver and rice exceeds one-half of the regular tax.

Zhejiang has suffered frequent disasters in recent years. The people's strength has been depleted, and the burden of taxes has become heavier, leading to more arrears. Officials and the people are in dire straits. The Chamber has repeatedly called for relief, and the Ministry of Finance has repeatedly ordered reductions, but the special tax has been designated for debt service and has not been reduced. The so-called debt service fund refers to the 18th year of the Republic construction bonds, which expired in the 28th year of the Republic. The people are already struggling to bear the burden. The newly revised Zhejiang Provincial Public Bond Regulations include the special tax in the principal and interest repayment items. The repayment period is divided into four types: fourteen years, sixteen years, eighteen years, and twenty years, extending the term of the original debt service fund by more than ten years. With repeated extensions, this harsh tax will never be abolished, and the people's difficulties will never be alleviated. Fortunately, Article 6 of the regulations states that if there are changes in the income designated for the fund before the public bonds are cleared, the Zhejiang Provincial Government shall request the approval of the Executive Yuan to designate other income, such as land tax, deed tax, and brokerage business tax, to fully supplement the amount. This can be used as a remedy after the fact. The Chamber respectfully asks the committee to have sympathy for the people's difficulties and to promptly send a letter to the Zhejiang Provincial Government to follow the original plan and stop the special construction tax when it expires in the 28th year of the Republic, without continuing it. Other funds should be designated to supplement the amount and announce this clearly to dispel public doubts. Although the Chamber understands the current difficult times and the provincial treasury's financial difficulties, it dares not insist on its previous view of a complete and immediate abolition. However, it requests that the tax be stopped on schedule in accordance with the previous plan, which will surely be appreciated. Furthermore, the provincial deed tax, brokerage business tax, etc., were previously listed as security for bonds but are not included in the new regulations' principal and interest repayment fund items. This is stated jointly. This is addressed to the Zhejiang Provincial Donation and Tax Supervision Committee, from the Zhejiang General Chamber of Commerce.

Gao Jianfu and Students' Art Exhibition: Preview for All Sectors Yesterday 113

Masterpiece "Battle of Shanghai" Planned for Municipal Museum Collection; Official Exhibition Opens Today Until the 28th

Lingnan renowned painter Gao Jianfu, professor at Zhongshan University and Central University, and his students Fang Rending, Wang Wenhao, Situ Qi, Wu Gonghu, Li Fuhong, He Bingguang, Ms. Wu Peirong, Ms. Yu Ruiyang, Ms. Yu Ruiyan, Ms. Liang Jingyun, Ms. Yang Yinbing, Ms. Zheng Danran, and 29 others, as well as ancient paintings from Gao's collection, totaling 242 pieces, opened at the International General Association on Jing'an Temple Road yesterday at 4:00 PM. Organizers Sun Ke and Wu Tiecheng, as well as guests from all sectors, including Feng Ziyou, Jian Youwen, Liu Haisu, Yi Dachang, and Liu Shi, Liang Xiaochu, and over a hundred others, attended the event. The exhibition will be held at the association from 10:00 AM today until 7:00 PM on the 28th.

Participating Works: The talented students of Gao Jianfu's Chunshui Painting Academy, which advocates for "Spring Awakening" publicly exhibited at the Nanjing Overseas Chinese Reception Center. Recently, it has been moved to the International General Association at 722 Jing'an Temple Road in this city. It is sponsored by Sun Ke of the Legislative Yuan, Cai Yuanpei, President of the Academia Sinica, Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of this city, and organizations such as the Chinese Women's Association, the China Review Society, the T'ien Hsia Monthly, the Cosmic Wind Society, the Yi Qiang Society, and the Chunshui Painting Academy. The total includes 66 works by Gao Jianfu, 3 works by Ms. Song Minghuang (Gao's wife), 3 works by Ms. Gao Lihua, and 100 works by Gao Jianfu's students, such as "Internal Conflict," "Battle of Shanghai," "After Plowing," and "Strengthen Our Air Defense," and the "Guangzhou Sun Yat-sen Memorial" are all masterpieces of their time.

Mayor's Report: At the preview yesterday afternoon, Mayor Wu introduced Gao Jianfu to the guests and gave an introductory speech, saying, "Mr. Gao Jianfu is a renowned Chinese painter. Gao's success lies in his perseverance and dedication to art, day after day for decades. He also went to Japan and India, adopting styles from various countries to complement his work, integrating them and forming his own style, truly worthy of being called a grand master of new Chinese painting. In recent years, he has also founded the Chunshui Painting Academy in Guangdong, which is also highly reputable. Today, the public exhibition of Gao's masterpieces and the works of his students is a great event for the art world."

Gao's Eloquent Discussion: Gao then spoke eloquently about Chinese painting, saying, "Today, I am honored that President Sun, President Cai, Mayor Wu, and the Chinese Women's Association, T'ien Hsia Society, Cosmic Wind Society, Yi Jing Society, China Review Society, and various cultural organizations are sponsoring this exhibition. I am also very grateful for the presence and guidance of guests from home and abroad. Unfortunately, the works of my colleagues are not very brilliant, and I am afraid that they will not meet the expectations of the refined audience. I am very ashamed and apologetic, and I hope for your expert guidance. Civilized countries in the world all know the relationship between art and life, so they all strive to promote and encourage it. Ancient China was the same. The Song Dynasty established a painting academy and even used painting to select officials. Chinese painting reached its peak during the Song Dynasty, with all methods perfected and all styles proficient, truly worthy of being called the golden age of Chinese art. Unfortunately, each generation after the Song Dynasty was worse than the previous, and now it can be said to be extremely declining. However, since the Republic of China, it seems that there is a glimmer of hope, a good omen of reversal. In general, the Chinese Renaissance will be at this time. I feel that the more developed the world's science is, the more rampant human desires become. If we do not vigorously practice Eastern art to harmonize with the spirit, I am afraid that mankind will not be able to enjoy the happiness of science. Because academic harmony is closely related to national harmony, I often feel that the art education in the world, both East and West, is somewhat biased. It seems necessary to harmonize, adopt, and exchange strengths. Eastern art emphasizes the void, while Western art emphasizes the real. Seeking reason from reality emphasizes scientific materialism. The good thing about Western painting is that it is truly in harmony with nature and assimilated to it. In recent decades, Western art has also had a tendency towards Easternization, and it is known the beauty of Eastern lines, but lines are only one method of constructing painting, only a part. Chinese painting emphasizes the essence of the spirit and is not limited to this. It needs to be based on literature, what is called learning from nature externally and obtaining the source from the heart internally, not focusing solely on skills and colors. For example, when painting landscapes, it is not enough to just paint a hill or a gully. One scene ends, and another scene arises, what is called 'When the mountains and rivers are exhausted and there seems to be no way out, the willows are dark and the flowers are bright, and there is another village.' Therefore, a painting is full of poetic meaning and philosophy, and the interest of calligraphy is in it. Sometimes, although there are only a few strokes, using ink sparingly, but this abstract beauty of the spirit that transcends the image can give the viewer a sense of beauty that is remaining and inexhaustible, like the meaning beyond the strings of music, the flavor beyond the taste of poetry, and the painting beyond the painting. Transmitting the spirit and conveying the meaning beyond the male and female orioles, bewildering and mysterious, profound and profound. We Eastern artists hold a view of life that is lofty and transcends the world. No matter how difficult the environment is, as long as there is a piece of paper, we can go to the world to depict all the sorrows of society. As long as there is a zither, we can play out our full of sorrow and indignation and infinite aspirations. Therefore, artists rarely violate their conscience because of material things. But in this evil world of the weak eating the strong and rampant desires, it seems that we should embrace the strengths of the Eastern artistic spirit and contribute it to the world as much as possible, like injecting an ampoule of tranquilizer. Moreover, beauty is a harmonizing agent of various relative qualities. We should broaden our vision, abandon the narrow Monroe Doctrine of Chinese painting, and expand it to the universalism of world art, so that art can be used to connect international emotions and to fully express the cruel and evil war and the sorrow of mankind, thereby promoting the world peace movement. I hope that weapons will be melted into the light of the sun and the moon. This is my earnest hope. If there are any mistakes in the works of my colleagues, I hope that you will give your guidance." After Gao finished his speech, his daughter Ms. Gao Lihua gave a report in English.

Famous Painting Collection: The Gao and students' art exhibition displays a total of 371 works. In addition to Gao's works, there are also works by his wife Ms. Song Minghuang, his daughter Ms. Gao Lihua, and his students Rong Dakui and Wu Gonghu, among others. Gao's works, "Wind and Rain Soaking Stallions," "Autumn Wind," and "Cold Forest Misty Barrier," are all considered masterpieces. His famous work "Battle of Shanghai" depicts the ruins of the Oriental Library, with blazing fire, especially able to make people deeply reflect. The municipal museum plans to collect it to commemorate it permanently.

China National Products Maintenance Association Sends Letter to Customs Requesting Release of National Products 118

Prove that Cloth from Da Hsin National Cloth Factory is a National Product; Please Investigate and Release Immediately to Facilitate the Sales of National Products

The China National Products Maintenance Association sent a letter to the Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs and the Inspector General of Customs, stating: "We are writing to you regarding the issue of releasing cloth from the Da Hsin Cloth Factory. We have received a letter from our member, the Da Hsin Cloth Factory in Tianjin, stating that a box of cloth stored at the closed port of the factory was shipped back to Shanghai on the Haiyuan ship on May 8th. However, the Jianghai Customs mistakenly identified it as foreign goods and required that duties be paid before it could be released. Although they submitted the factory's and Hong Kong's cargo ledgers, sample trademarks, and national product certificate, the customs has not approved the release. We are therefore writing to request that your association forward a letter to the Jianghai Customs to certify that the goods are national products and to release them promptly to facilitate the sales of national products. After reviewing the factory's details, we found that the factory is located at Jiangyi Hutong, Houjiahou, Tianjin, and has been selling various cloths with the hexagonal 'Zhongxin' trademark throughout the country for many years. The factory has been verified by the factory association and found to be in compliance with the national product standards promulgated by the Ministry of Industry, and has been issued National Product Certificate No. 111. The goods shipped back to Shanghai this time from the factory's Hong Kong warehouse consist of 30 yards of worsted wool for ten pieces, 30 yards of Xiangfei plaid for ten pieces, and three pieces of canvas, all packed in one box. There is no doubt that they are national products. Therefore, we are sending this special letter with attached trademarks, samples, and the certificate to certify that the cloth is indeed a national product manufactured by the factory. We earnestly request your customs office to instruct the relevant departments to investigate and release the goods to benefit the sales of national products. We are deeply grateful for your public-spiritedness."

Economics Society Offers Reward for Essays 120

The Chinese Economics Society is offering a prize for essays on national economic construction plans. The advertisement has been widely published in major newspapers, and there has been an enthusiastic response from all sectors. Because the summer vacation is approaching, it is most convenient for university professors and students to write essays during the holidays. The society has printed and sent the rules for participation to universities and specialized schools across the country to post them on campus to publicize the event. It is reported that the essays should be between 10,000 and 20,000 words and can be written in either vernacular or classical Chinese. However, the plans must be concrete and feasible. Participants are not limited to university faculty, students, or members of the society. For detailed rules and regulations, please inquire by mail to Shanghai Post Office Box 4019 or Nanjing Post Office Box 252, to the society's Essay Committee.

Iron Department Approves Incentives for Transporting Domestically Produced Porcelain 121

Effective July 1st

Railway Bureau News: In the past, to encourage the transportation of domestically produced porcelain from Jiangxi via railway, the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau drafted "Measures for Packaging, Transportation, and Incentives for Jiangxi Domestically Produced Porcelain" and submitted it to the Ministry of Railways. The Ministry ordered the Bureau to jointly draft special through rates. Both parties carefully discussed the matter and, referring to the original measures proposed by the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway, stipulated that "Jiangxi domestically produced porcelain transported via the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway will be charged at the third-class rate if packaged in crates or barrels. All other forms of packaging for Jiangxi domestically produced porcelain will be charged at the fifth-class rate." This was established as a special through rate and applied the "distance reduction" method for through freight, so that domestically produced porcelain from other places with different packaging would not be affected. Furthermore, as the sales range of Jiangxi domestically produced porcelain is very wide, it was proposed that the above-mentioned special through rate should be uniformly applied by all connecting railways. This was jointly submitted to the Ministry for approval by the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway. Now, the Ministry Order No. 5506 states, "Approval is granted to proceed accordingly, effective from July 1st. However, these measures are only a specific method for distinguishing the grades of Jiangxi domestically produced porcelain based on packaging methods and are not limited to application on these two railways. Moreover, when through transport from Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway to other railways occurs, the 'distance reduction' method shall naturally apply, but it shall not be referred to as a special through rate." The Bureau has already instructed the Transportation Department to comply accordingly.

Lawyers Prohibited from Practicing Law in County Governments Concurrently Handling Judicial Affairs 122

The Shanghai Bar Association issued a notice to all members yesterday, which stated: "We hereby notify you that we have received Instruction No. 9987 from the Jiangsu Higher Court, stating: 'The practice of law by lawyers should be conducted in ordinary courts, as stipulated in Article 1 of the Lawyers' Regulations. They may not practice law in county governments that concurrently handle judicial affairs. This has also been interpreted and recorded in Supreme Court Resolution No. 123 of the 17th year of the Republic. However, it has recently been found that some lawyers have established offices in areas under county governments that concurrently handle judicial affairs, employing clerks to solicit lawsuits or even serving as legal advisors to local merchants and residents, advertising widely, and engaging in promotion. Such conduct is inconsistent with the aforementioned laws and regulations and is highly inappropriate. In addition to separately ordering the counties that concurrently handle judicial affairs to investigate and prohibit such activities, we hereby order your association to notify all members to comply strictly and pay close attention to this matter.' Upon receipt of this, a corresponding letter is sent to you for your information and compliance."

Fire at Zhongxing Road, Zhabei 124

Firefighters Injured During Brave Rescue Efforts

The Fengnian Senji Dyeing and Weaving Factory, located at No. 23 to No. 25 Beizhufan Lane, Zhongxing Road, Zhabei, is owned by Kan Peisheng from Anhui Province. Yesterday afternoon around 4:00 PM, a fire suddenly broke out on the ground floor of the factory, quickly spreading throughout. Flames soared, and the fire also spread to the neighboring Tongsheng Cloth Factory at No. 22. At the time, the fire illuminated the sky and was uncontrollable. Fortunately, the fire brigades from various sections of Zhabei had received the alert and rushed fire engines to the scene to attempt to extinguish the fire, preventing further spread. The fire was completely extinguished after about an hour. As a result, four buildings were burned down. Kan Peisheng, the owner of the factory where the fire originated, was taken to the Zhongxing Road Police Station for questioning. However, during the height of the fire, Sun Shengshen, a 30-year-old firefighter from the Hongzhen District Fire Brigade, saw the raging fire and fearlessly rushed to the rescue. He carelessly fell from a height, injuring his head and losing consciousness on the spot. He was quickly transported to the hospital by ambulance for treatment and regained consciousness. His injuries are not considered serious.

Soaring Tung Oil Exports 125

U.S. Imports Exceeded Several Million Dollars Last Period

Dagong News Agency: According to the International Trade Bureau, the Ministry of Commerce's simplified chemical examination report stated that exports had increased by 70% compared to previous periods. The total consumption in 1935 was 127,600,000 pounds. This tung oil almost entirely came from China, with only a small amount supplied by the Gulf Coast of the United States. Other new tung oil industries are gradually emerging. Based on the average price of 18 cents per pound this year, the tung oil used by the American paint industry in 1936 accounted for about 75% of the total value. The total consumption in 1935 was 98,440,000 pounds. The oilcloth industry ranked second, with a consumption of 10,390,000 pounds in 1935, a significant increase compared to 7,300,000 pounds in 1932. The paint industry used a total of 2,003,000 pounds of tung oil last year, compared to 713,000 pounds in 1932. In 1935, the consumption by other industries totaled 10,756,000 pounds, compared to 7,892,000 pounds in 1932. The tung oil used by the electrical industry, the plywood industry, waterproofing compounds, automotive fabrics, and raincoat manufacturing is also considerable. According to other news, tung oil exports have been very good in the first half of this year. U.S. sales reached over ten million dollars, an increase compared to the same period last year. Exports to other countries such as England, Germany, France, and Italy have also been active. Therefore, there is still much hope for the future of tung oil exports.

Land Officials Accused of Extortion Case Tried Yesterday 126

Both Sides Present Evidence

The case of Shanghai Land Bureau Second Technology Section Chief Ye Changfu and Technician Zhang Zhenfan, accused by citizen Han Qixiang of extorting 1,200 yuan for upgrading land plans, was tried yesterday by Judge Wu after being prosecuted by the District Court Prosecutor. The defendants Ye Changfu and Zhang Zhenfan, represented by a lawyer, argued in court that Han Qixiang, also known as Jin Tucheng, had applied for an exemption from upgrading the land plans for the 451st base within the Over-the-word Embankment in the 25th Bao district, claiming that there were errors in the road plan. However, the chief and technician were acting on instructions from the Third Section, and approval or rejection was up to the section chief. The road was to be upgraded, and it had been verified and confirmed as a settled case during the tenure of the previous bureau director in the 23rd year of the Republic. There was no possibility of seeking bribes, and this was clearly inconsistent with the facts. Han Qixiang claimed that he dined at the Quanxingkang Hotel and had a menu as proof, but the food on the menu could be obtained by anyone and could not serve as evidence. Han Qiqiang claimed that Wang and Lu, two friends, were present at the banquet at the Quanxingkang Hotel. If they were friends in attendance, why did he not know their names and addresses? This was not truthful and was clearly a false accusation due to unmet requests. Han Qixiang also claimed that he contacted a man named Tao Asheng to apply for a land business license, who said that a bribe of 1,200 yuan was required, which would include the upgrading of land. He had tea at Yile Tian and dined at Quanxingkang Hotel, but because negotiations failed, his rights were harmed. The judge stated that since both sides had evidence, he would summon witnesses for a retrial.

Female Flower Association Kingpin Lu Laoqi Imprisoned 127

Knowing It Was Inevitable, She Reported to the Court

Lu Laoqi, also known as Wenying, the female kingpin of the Flower Association, was previously wanted by the French Concession Police Department through the Second Special District Court. Last winter, Inspector Qian Chenglong and detectives from the Old Zhabei Police Station captured Lu in Yuren Lane in the Public Concession and brought her to the Second Special District Court. The Legal Affairs Office of the Police Department prosecuted her according to law. After trial, she was sentenced to one year and six months of penal servitude and fined 2,000 yuan. During the appeal period, she posted a bond of 6,000 yuan with a shop as guarantor. Later, because Lu did not accept the original judgment, she appealed to the Third Branch of the Higher Court. As a result, the original sentence was reduced by six months, and she was sentenced to one year of penal servitude. However, the fine portion remained at the original 2,000 yuan. Recently, the Second Branch of the Higher Court finalized the case and summoned Lu to report for execution of the sentence. Lu submitted a petition claiming illness and requesting a postponement, which was rejected by the court. The guarantor was ordered to bring Lu to the case. Knowing that it was unavoidable, Lu voluntarily reported to the Third Branch of the Higher Court the day before yesterday and was interrogated by the executing judge. The bailiffs were ordered to send her to the prison for execution.

Woman Commits Adultery with Brother-in-Law, Arrested and Expresses Repentance to Husband 128

However, Forgiveness Is Not Granted; Case Concluded and Awaiting Judgment

Yang Meixing, a local man, is 28 years old and resides at No. 2 Yangjia House, Huangxing Road, Zhabei. He used to work as a comprador on a ship but is now unemployed. Yang previously married Ms. Xu (23 years old this year) and lives with her. They have children. Yang's elder sister is married to Tan Yunjun (25 years old this year), a local man residing at No. 25 Kangnao Road. Tan works at the Free Farm. Yang's wife, Ms. Xu, is naturally frivolous. Starting from the first month of the lunar calendar last year, she had an affair with her husband's brother-in-law, Tan Yunjun. She often used excuses to go out and secretly meet at hotels, engaging in secret rendezvous for more than a year. Yang and his sister were completely unaware. On the 21st, Yang's wife, Ms. Xu, went to the home of relatives at No. 2 Sanxin Lane, Caishi Road, in the French Concession. She had arranged with Tan to meet at the entrance of the Central Cinema at 6:00 PM that day and go to a hotel for further pleasure. At 6:00 PM that afternoon, Ms. Xu came out of Sanxin Lane and took a trolleybus to the Central Cinema to wait for Tan. Tan was already waiting. After the two met, they went to a restaurant on Avenue Dubail for dinner. At 7:00 PM, they went to the Dadong New Hotel at No. 94 Xixinqiao Street and opened Room 107 for illicit intercourse. Unexpectedly, their good fortune was short-lived. Yang's and Ms. Xu's trip to the hotel was spotted by Yang Meixing's friend Hu Shiquan (28 years old, local man), who tailed them to the hotel and immediately reported to Yang.

Yang immediately rushed to the French Concession Police Department to report. Detectives were dispatched to the Dadong New Hotel to arrest them. At the time, the adulterer and adulteress were both naked in bed. The detectives ordered them to get dressed and took them to the police station for detention. The next day, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court. Lawyer Yuan Jiahuang from the Police Affairs Office presented the case, prosecuting them for the crime of disrupting the family. Then, the plaintiff, Yang Meixing, complained that the defendants had committed adultery and requested strict investigation. The court declared that the case involved morality and announced that onlookers were prohibited. It was heard that the defendants admitted to having committed adultery for a long time. Ms. Xu Yang repented to her husband in court, asking the court for leniency, but the plaintiff did not grant it. The court ordered the conclusion of the debate and set the judgment for the 29th. The defendants were sent back to detention.

Mother Also Conspired; All Involved Arrested

After Qiu Chunshan Was Slashed, The Culprit Distributed Leaflets 130

Falsely Claiming to Be Patriotic Youth Association; Qiu Has Presented It to the Court for Thorough Investigation

Qiu Chunshan, from Zhenjiang, has been in Shanghai for over 20 years. He is the chairman of the city's rickshaw association, the supervisor of the Chunhua Silk Edging Factory's union, and a representative to the city's Chamber of Commerce. He is a well-known member of the middle class. A few days ago, he was suddenly assassinated in a deserted area west of the South Railway Station, suffering five axe wounds and nearly dying. The Municipal Public Security Bureau sent him to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. While the matter was being investigated, the culprits distributed leaflets falsely claiming that the Patriotic Youth Association was behind the attack. Qiu believes that the assault and the leaflets were the work of the same person and has learned that it was motivated by jealousy from a competitor seeking to replace him. He has presented a petition to the District Court for thorough investigation.
