Ruling on Compensation for Bloodshed at the Continental Ballroom 131

Chen Weiling Suffered Significant Injury; Liang Shaoqian Must Pay Over a Thousand Gold

Chen Weiling, an employee of the Dazhonghang on Henan Road, had a conflict with Liang Shaoqian, a Cantonese employee of the Continental Ballroom, late on the night of April 10th. As a result, Chen's left wrist was slashed with a knife, and the bone was broken. The police arrested Liang and handed him over to the First Special District Court, which sentenced Liang to eight months of penal servitude with a three-year reprieve. Chen's incidental civil suit was transferred to the civil court. Chen then hired lawyer Jiang Chiping to file a civil suit with the Civil Division of the First Special District Court, seeking compensation for damages and medical expenses, totaling over 7,200 yuan. Because Chen's hand has been disabled since the injury and he can no longer work, the court ordered a medical assessment, which found that although Chen's injury did not reach the level of disability, he had lost one-third of his working ability. Judge Li Hu, who presided over the trial, ordered Liang Shaoqian to compensate Chen Weiling for damages and medical expenses in the amount of 1,036.80 national currency yesterday morning.

Public Education Center Establishes Special Inquiry Office for Smokers 132

Since the Municipal Public Security Bureau began registering smokers, many smokers who did not understand the anti-smoking laws have gone to the bureau to inquire. There has also been a constant stream of people requesting to quit smoking and obtaining smoking cessation registration forms. To facilitate smokers' inquiries about anti-smoking laws and to obtain smoking cessation registration forms, the bureau consulted with the Public Education Center of the Confucius Temple Park and specially allocated a room to establish a smoker inquiry office. The internal arrangements have been completed, and the office officially opened yesterday. The bureau's public notice for the establishment of the smoker inquiry office is copied below: "In order to guide smokers on registration procedures and to clarify the anti-smoking laws, the bureau has established a smoker registration inquiry office in the Nanshi Public Education Center (Confucius Temple Park). It will open for business on the 23rd of this month. Citizens who are unclear about registration, licensing, smoking cessation procedures, or anti-smoking laws should go to the office to inquire. We will provide detailed answers. This is hereby announced."

Shi Yu Gao, Stranded in Shanghai, Hangs Himself in Seclusion Late at Night 133

Near the Nanshi Cemetery Pier, a young man suddenly appeared at around 12:00 AM last night, wearing a blue cloth shirt and pants, standing alone in a secluded spot. After looking around and seeing no one, he untied the hemp rope from his waist and tied it to the high railing of the wooden fence, then put the noose around his neck, intending to hang himself. At that moment, Chen Amao, a boatman on a sampan docked at the pier, saw the scene and was greatly alarmed. He jumped ashore and cut the man down. Because it had not been long, he was saved. He reported to the Shanghai Municipal Water Patrol. After questioning by the team leader, the man said his name was Shi Yu Gao, 18 years old, from Minhou County. His brother, Yu Shi, is a second-class soldier on the Xianning warship. They came to Shanghai together the day before yesterday, but he got lost near Xiaodongmen. The warship had already sailed to Nanjing, and he was stranded in a foreign land with no relatives. He had no choice but to attempt suicide. Team Leader Wei, based on the statement, felt pity for him and has submitted a request to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to provide assistance.

Fifteen Stores Warned; No Such Person as "Modern Young Master" 134

Zhang Ye'er of the Mental Troupe Pulled a Prank; Zhou Xiangsheng Startled Upon Seeing Newspaper

The previous day, all the local newspapers published an advertisement warning "Modern Young Master" Yan Runfu, listing fifteen creditors, including Xiangsheng Automobile Company and Hongxiang Fashion Company. Because the wording of the advertisement was serious, readers suspected that Yan Runfu actually existed. The creditors listed above, such as Xiangsheng Automobile Company, also had misunderstandings, suspecting that their store names had been falsely listed. A reporter from Datong News Agency has revealed the truth: Zhang Ye'er, the protagonist of the Mental Troupe performing at the New World Company, is preparing to perform the play "Modern Young Master" on the 30th of this month at the Xinguang Grand Theater. To attract attention, he created a false impression by publishing the advertisement. However, he did not contact the creditors listed in the advertisement beforehand. Zhou Xiangsheng, the manager of Xiangsheng Automobile Company, discovered the advertisement the previous morning and was very concerned. Later, Zhang Ye'er sent a clerk to notify him, and he was relieved. This is also an amusing anecdote.

French School Apprehends Young Book Thief 135

Shi Xinlou, a young man from Shaoxing, wandered around Shanghai with no occupation. Recently, due to the pressure of life, he had a whimsical idea. Dressed as a student, he used the guise of visiting schoolmates to sneak into dormitories to steal. At around 8:00 AM the day before yesterday, Shi again sneaked into the Sino-French School near Baxianqiao in the French Concession, intending to steal students' books (since the school had no dormitories, all students were day students). He was spotted by a teacher, Father (priest), who suspected that Shi was not a student of the school and looked suspicious. Also, four students, including Ge Hua ran, had their expensive French books stolen a few days ago. He detained Shi and called the police. According to Shi's confession, he stole eight books and sold them to Dafeng and Shan Ye bookstores on Zhonghua Road in Nanshi to get money. Detective Xu Daorong took Shi to the Dafeng Bookstore to retrieve six of the original books. The two books received by the Shan Ye Bookstore had already been resold to others and could not be retrieved. Yesterday, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court. The Police Affairs Office lawyer requested an adjournment for investigation and prosecution. Judge Chen Pusheng verified the report and briefly questioned the defendant, ordering a retrial at a later date. The defendant was returned to custody.

Careless Cooking of Zongzi Causes Fire Spreading to Multiple Homes 136

At 6:12 AM yesterday morning, a fire broke out at the front building of the Lin Faji Sofa Shop at No. 18 Taian Lane, North Shanxi Road, due to careless cooking of zongzi. Thick smoke billowed, and flames spread rapidly. The Central Fire Brigade dispatched a belt-driven fire engine to the scene. It took several hours to extinguish the fire. In addition to No. 18 being completely burned down, the fire also spread to the upstairs of five other shops: the Chen family at No. 20, the Zhu family at No. 16, Renyu Iron Shop at No. 14, Tongdexing Clothing Shop, the Wang family at No. 12, and Feng Jin Tai Tailor shop No. 10. The fire starter was arrested by street police and taken to the police station for investigation.

Wuxi Girl Lured to Shanghai for Prostitution 137

Mother Shouted in the Streets to Find Her Daughter; Many Shady Details Awaiting Further Investigation

Jiang Zhai, a 37-year-old woman from Wuxi, lives in the countryside of Wuxi. Her husband died of illness six years ago, leaving behind two daughters, the elder named Jisheng, 16 years old, and the younger named Aisheng, 13 years old. However, since the death of her husband, Jiang Zhai, not accustomed to sleeping alone, became involved with Wang Laoer (i.e., Jiang Xianzai). Jiang Aisheng had a foster father named Lu Jinsong who, last year, under the pretext of recommending her for factory work, brought Aisheng from Wuxi to Shanghai. On the 29th of last month, Lu Jinsong suddenly went to Jiang Zhai's home in Wuxi, saying that Aisheng was seriously ill in Shanghai and that Jisheng needed

to visit her.

Jiang Zhai did not know his plan. She had her eldest daughter Jisheng follow Lu to Shanghai. Unexpectedly, Lu secretly colluded with Wang Laoer, Gao Laoqi, etc., and forced Jiang Jisheng into a prostitute house opened by Zhang Asi, a Yangzhou native, at No. 18 Hongxiang Lane, No. 57 Xinzha Road. They set a four-year term and got 181 yuan as her starting price. From then on, Jiang Jisheng fell into the fiery pit, renamed Xiaomei. Every night, Zhang Asi dispatched a maid to accompany her to the rooftop garden of Wing On Company

to solicit customers.

The money earned each night was managed by Zhang. For several days, the Jiang girl,

unable to bear the pain,

escaped privately late one night while the accompanying maid was not paying attention. She went to live temporarily at the home of a fellow villager. But after Jiang girl disappeared, Zhang Asi negotiated with Lu Jinsong, etc. Lu and Wang Laoer, etc., tried to find Jiang Jisheng and sent her to the home of Cai Shunhai, a Changzhou native, at No. 87 Arrabella Street

for surveillance. Unexpectedly,

the matter was discovered by Jiang Zhai, who arrived in Shanghai by train yesterday

to find her daughter

directly to the area of Arrabella Street. Because she did not know the house number, she shouted her daughter Jisheng's name along the way. Jisheng heard her, eagerly stuck her head out of the building window, and greeted each other. Ms. Jiang entered the house to take Jisheng away, but she was stopped by Cai Shunhai, causing a conflict and chaos. Hua Police No. 458 saw this and brought Jiang Zhai, Jiang Jisheng, and Cai Shunhai

to the Huishi Police Station,

where they learned the details and transferred them to the Xinzha Police Station. Chinese detective Yang Fusheng went to No. 18 Hongxiang Lane, Xinwen Road, to arrest Zhang Asi and his son Zhang Yusheng (18 years old) together

at the police station

for detention. Yesterday morning, Police Station Lawyer Zhang Tianyin charged Zhang Asi and his son with the crime of disrupting the family under Article 203 of the Criminal Code, and Cai Shunhai with the crime of restricting freedom under Article 300 of the Criminal Code. The content of this case is complicated, and Lu Jinsong was captured this morning, so he requested permission to postpone the trial. Also, according to Jiang Zhai and Jiang Jisheng, who successively surrendered, the above situation was explained. When asked about Zhang Asi, he admitted that he spent 181 yuan to buy Jiang Jisheng as an adopted daughter. At first, he wanted her to

learn to dance.

Later, because he knew that Jiang was not a virgin and because she voluntarily took up the life of a goddess, he accompanied her to public places to receive guests. Unexpectedly, Jiang girl ran away privately after only three days. It was discovered that Tu Laoer's real name was Jiang Xianzai, who was a pigeon keeper by trade, and that he really used fraudulent means to

obtain my money, etc.

Zhang Yusheng said that he serves as

a set designer

I have nothing to do with this matter and hired lawyer Fan Gang to defend him, stating that there were many shady details in this case and that the master criminal, Wang Laoer, could not be captured, so it should

allow bail.

Cai Shunhai said that Jiang Jisheng was sent to my place by Wang Laoer et al. for temporary residence, and I don't know anything else. After Judge Tan Zheng verified the statement, the court ordered that the case be retried on the 26th. Zhang Yusheng, Cai Shunhai, Jiang Zhai, and Jiang Jisheng were each released

with guarantees. Zhang Asi was returned to custody.

Zhang Hebo's Deceased Concubine's Immoral Conduct: The Principal Wife Worries About Her Son 138

Sues to Revoke the Concubine's Guardianship Rights; Jurisdiction Issues Require Investigation

Zhang Hebo, a wealthy merchant from Wuxian County, Suzhou, married Yao Shuhui as his principal wife and later took Yuanru as a concubine. Zhang Hebo passed away from illness twelve years ago. At the time, Li was pregnant and had not yet given birth. After Zhang's death, she gave birth to a son named Yi Xin, who is now thirteen years old. Li has been raising him, but recently, Li has been found to be immoral. Zhang Yao Shuhui is concerned about the harm this may cause to Yi Xin's future education. Therefore, she retained lawyers Chen Tingrui and Xu Yinlu to file a lawsuit against Li Yuanru in the First Special District Court, citing Articles 1090 and 1094, Clause 5 of the Civil Code and Precedent No. 1974 of the Supreme Court in the 20th year of the Republic, requesting a judgment to terminate her guardianship of Yi Xin and to allow the plaintiff to convene a family council to select a new guardian. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Dai Rongduo of the Civil Court No. 14 summoned the parties. The defendant also retained lawyer Wang Chuanbi to defend her case, raising a jurisdictional issue, stating that the defendant currently resides at No. 104 Hulong Street, Suzhou, so the plaintiff should file the lawsuit with the Wuxian County Court, requesting a preliminary ruling. Plaintiff's lawyer Chen Tingrui stated that since Zhang Hebo's death, the defendant had remarried to a man named Li Dingsheng (also known as Zhiyun), who initially lived on Yunnan Road, then moved to No. 8 Guanhua Lane, Lafayette Road, and in early November of last year, moved to No. 122 Chibang Road, and recently resides at No. 10, Lane 652, Xinzha Road. Furthermore, the summons was delivered by the plaintiff and received by Li Dingsheng, indicating that the defendant does reside in Shanghai, so there is no jurisdictional issue. The court immediately announced that the defendant's summons had been returned to the court by Li Dingsheng with a letter, which was handed to lawyer Chen. The letter claimed that he and Li Yuanru were siblings. Lawyer Chen presented a photo of Li Dingsheng, Li Yuanru, and Zhang Yi Xin together, as well as letters, to prove that they were indeed husband and wife. After review, the judge ruled that an investigation was needed to verify jurisdiction. Therefore, the case was adjourned for further hearing.

The 15th Hygiene Campaign: Guiding Children's Lives Today 139

Yesterday was Factory Hygiene Day; Speech Contests to be Held Regularly

The 15th Shanghai Hygiene Campaign designated yesterday as Factory Hygiene Day, organized by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. Representatives from various factories in the city attended. Today is Children's Life Guidance Day. The Municipal People's Education Center is working hard to support this hygiene campaign. Details are as follows:

Yesterday's Factory Hygiene: Yesterday was Factory Hygiene Day, organized by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. At 1:00 PM, representatives from various factories were gathered in the Minglun Hall of the Municipal People's Education Center to attend a lecture. Sun Yongyi presided over the meeting and gave a brief report. Then, Li Xuanguo, Director of the Wusong Hygiene Office, delivered a lecture on factory hygiene. The meeting adjourned at 3:00 PM. Yesterday, celebrities were also invited to broadcast on various radio stations: Cai Hongtian from 4:00 to 4:30 PM on the Sino-Western station, Liu Zhanen from 4:50 to 5:10 PM on the Gospel station, and Weng Zhilong from 5:30 to 6:00 PM on the Municipal Government station.

Today Guiding Children: Today is Children's Life Guidance Day, organized by the Municipal People's Education Center. Starting at 1:00 PM, the center will send staff to perform various programs. Guo Qiyuan, Chen Tiesheng, and Jiang Hao will be invited to broadcast on various radio stations, and the News Evening Post will publish a special hygiene supplement.

Achievements of the Municipal People's Education Center: The hygiene exhibition is being held at the People's Education Center, so the center is responsible for many events, such as: 1. Adding a summer hygiene exhibition room. All arrangements are divided into: (A) The emergence and breeding of mosquitoes, from the arrangement of sewage to the emergence of mosquitoes and how to eliminate them. The process is displayed with real objects. (B) The emergence and breeding of flies, from the arrangement of garbage cans to the breeding of flies and how to eliminate them. A three-dimensional model of fly reproduction is used to show the quantity and speed of fly reproduction. (C) Preventing flies from contacting food, with clean food and food exposed to flies displayed side by side. (D) Summer hygiene in the bedroom, using beds, sundries, and medicines to display how to eliminate bedbugs. 2. Conducting epidemic prevention injections. Initially, the center's contracted doctors provided free cholera and typhoid vaccinations to the general public. As the weather became warmer this month, the number of visitors to the center increased sharply. Therefore, the center consulted with the Health Bureau, which sent staff to the center to administer injections daily. To date, more than 12,000 people have been vaccinated. 3. Conducting hygiene knowledge tests. The center cooperates with the Wuzhou Pharmacy. The method is to make the questions and methods as simple as possible to ensure that the tests are widely available. Anyone over the age of 16 who is literate and can write can participate. The tests are divided into three sessions: one at 5:00 PM on June 21st, one at 5:00 PM on June 22nd, and the last one at 5:00 PM on June 24th. 4. Holding hygiene campaign riddles, using summer hygiene knowledge as the material, and publicly soliciting guesses. 5. Holding a hygiene campaign speech contest, using the speech contest as a method and publicizing hygiene as the purpose, scheduled to be held publicly on the 28th of this month.

Ningbo Old Pontoon Bridge: Opening Ceremony Scheduled (Shanghai News) 140

The Ningbo Old Pontoon Bridge, also known as the Old Jiang Bridge or Ling Bridge in ancient times, has been in disrepair for many years and is quite dangerous. Two years ago, Ningbo gentlemen in Shanghai, including Jin Ting, Zhang Jiguang, and Le Zhenbao, initiated a reconstruction project. The Shanghai Municipal Council engineer, Cham, designed the bridge, and Siemens was contracted to build it. The entire bridge is made of steel, and the cost, including demolition and land concession fees, is estimated to be around 700,000 yuan. The project has taken several years and is now complete. The bridge is arched, tall, and sturdy, making it the greatest engineering project in Ningbo. It is said that the opening ceremony will be held on the 27th of this month, and the organizers will host a reception at the Xinning Shao Steamer on the 26th (the day before), which is expected to be a lively event.

Central Bank Inspection Report 144

The 288th Inspection Report on the Issuance Reserve of the Central Bank Exchange Certificates states: In accordance with Article 13 of the Central Bank Law, this committee is responsible for inspecting the number of exchange certificates issued by the bank and the reserve funds. The 288th inspection was conducted at the Issuance Bureau of the bank on June 20, 1936. The results of the inspection are reported as follows: (A) Total value of exchange certificates issued: 29,839,666.23 silver dollars, including 26,759,455.57 silver dollar certificates and 3,080,206.66 fractional currency certificates. Total value of exchange certificate reserves: 29,839,666.23 silver dollars, including 20,121,672.23 silver dollars in cash reserve. The cash reserve includes 11,272,777.9571 silver dollars stored in the bank's issuing headquarters, branch warehouses, and branches, and 8,848,892.729 silver dollars stored in correspondent banks. Guarantee reserves total 9,717,993.00 silver dollars. (B) Total value of cash exchange certificates issued: 400,963.07 Customs Gold Units. Total value of Customs Gold Unit exchange certificate reserves: 400,963.07 Customs Gold Units. The reserve includes 7,926.290 ounces of pure gold, valued at 51.68 Customs Gold Units per ounce, totaling 400,963.07 Customs Gold Units. In accordance with Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve should be at least 60%, with the remainder as a guarantee reserve of legally acceptable goods. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is within 40%, which complies with the law. This report is hereby submitted. June 22, 1936, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank: Li Fusun, Supervisors: Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Ji.

Weather Report 154

The Shanghai Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: Shandong, the middle reaches of the Yangtze River, and the area of Hankou will be clear and hot with southeast to southwest winds. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River and this area will have southeast winds and may experience thunder. The East China Sea and Taiwan will change from cloudy to overcast with southeast to southwest winds and localized fog. There is a low-pressure area southeast of Mindanao. Also, within 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in Shanghai reached a high of 87.6 and a low of 71.4. On the same day last year, the high was 78.4 and the low was 68.7.

The Shenbao National Goods Special Issue

Contributing to the Nanyang Commercial Survey Group 155

— Xuan Wan

According to reports, the Shanghai China Industrial Foreign Trade Association has recently organized a Nanyang Commercial Survey Group to actively promote domestic products for export, open up foreign markets, and develop overseas trade. It has been decided that starting from the 3rd of next month, groups will depart to various places in Nanyang – Manila, Surabaya, Batavia, Singapore, Penang, Saigon, Siam, Medan, and other places – to conduct surveys, and will carry a large number of domestic product samples and specimens to distribute to various places for promotion, and to establish close ties with the local business community, which is a precursor to the promotion of domestic products overseas.

In the current situation where the entire domestic product sector is struggling through stormy conditions, we are indeed happy to hear this encouraging news. We know that in the past and present, there are many compatriots overseas, especially in various parts of Nanyang, who are eagerly longing for the motherland and demanding domestic products. Therefore: We are bound to receive a grand welcome on this trip, but on the other hand, we must ensure that we completely satisfy them. I hope that the members of the survey group will work hard to fulfill the pioneering mission and conduct practical work, especially paying attention to the following three points: Now, I write down these words as my small contribution:

First, expand publicity. The Nanyang region has originally been occupied by foreign goods, and there are many compatriots there who truly want to use domestic products but cannot obtain them. Therefore, we must expand publicity for domestic products on this trip, and pay attention to the production of advertisements and commodity samples, so that they first have a deep impression of domestic products, and at the same time, understand the principles of Chinese people applying domestic goods, so that everyone loves to use domestic products.

Second, establish permanent exhibition halls. After our trip, we should take advantage of the enthusiastic goodwill of compatriots from all walks of life towards domestic products, and take a further step to plan the establishment of permanent domestic product exhibition halls there, so that the local residents and vendors can have a more adequate understanding, and can continue to subscribe from domestic product manufacturers in Shanghai.

Third, solve various difficult problems. The reason why domestic products could not be sold to Nanyang in the past was because many technical difficulties hindered them. This time, we must work together with the local business community to obtain appropriate solutions to problems such as packaging, shipping and bank financing, and currency system budgeting for exchange rates, in order to facilitate the future development and progress of trade.

Words of Contribution

Strengthening Trade Associations 157

— Yang An

To seek the development of China's domestic industrial goods, nothing is better than strengthening trade associations. The revision of the Law of Industrial and Commercial Trade Associations is particularly urgent. Recently, the Legislative Yuan's Ministry of Industry has proposed amendments to the Law of Industrial and Commercial Trade Associations. An important resolution of the 7th Member Representative Assembly of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, for strengthening the organization of merchant groups, that businesses must join the trade association, and trade associations must join the Chamber of Commerce, has been unanimously approved by the assembly. At this time, before the amended laws are promulgated, we should make seven preparations:

1. If there is no trade association, organize one as soon as possible to unify the purpose of the industry and standardize the steps of the industry.

2. After the trade association is organized, for those in the industry who have not joined, investigate and persuade them to join, so as to gather ideas and cooperate in case of trouble. Otherwise, as limited by laws and regulations, sooner or later they will not be able to stay outside the association and undermine the industry's front.

3. In addition to industrial and commercial trade associations, export trade associations should be organized to be a prelude to the development of foreign trade.

4. In addition to the Chamber of Commerce Law, the government should be asked to promulgate an Industrial Association Law, based on industrial trade associations, so that the industrial sector has a sound organization.

5. Trade associations should begin preparing for a strict organization with unified methods for tasks such as appraisal, inspection, statistics, production, and sales.

6. Amidst rampant smuggling, trade associations should strengthen defenses and take responsibility for inspecting products. If smuggled goods are found, they should be immediately seized to protect the industry.

The above is what our domestic goods industry should actively prepare for, and I hope that our government authorities will promote it as soon as possible to save the domestic goods industry from the brink of extinction.

The Need for Domestic Rubber Bands 158

— Yu Feng

The "rubber bands" I am talking about now are the rubber bands used by major department stores, shops, and pharmacies on Nanjing Road for bundling things. Because these rubber bands can be adjusted to be tight or loose, they are simple and convenient. They are better than linen thread and gauze ribbons. And their value is very low, not much different from linen thread and gauze ribbons. Therefore, it is more convenient to use rubber bands than to use linen thread and printed gauze ribbons. Therefore, most new-style large companies and large stores use rubber bands to bundle things.

Speaking of rubber bands, I have some feelings! According to a friend of mine who specializes in the stationery business, "Most of these rubber bands are of inferior quality. They sell very well in stationery supplies. The annual loss is not small..." From this point of view, it is just that the general small industrial sector and rubber manufacturers are not paying attention.

Japan is originally the most developed industrial country. Especially for daily necessities, creation and imitation can be described as meticulous. Chinese people in our industrially backward country have always loved foreign goods. How can they not be happy to use cheap and good goods? Now they supply us with simple and convenient rubber bands. In this atmosphere of serious "smuggling," these things are even cheaper. This makes us abandon domestic linen thread and gauze ribbons and become their loyal salesmen. In this "Civilian Domestic Goods Year," there is no shortage of domestic rubber manufacturers with foresight. Hurry up and imitate them to stop this trickle of loss. Don't think it is "small" and not worth caring about. You must know that in today's poverty-stricken Chinese social economy, we must have the "determination" not to buy foreign goods anymore! Otherwise, what about the "Women's Domestic Goods Year" that has been shouted hoarsely for the past few years? ... Isn't its effect equal to zero? If this continues, the social economic panic will lead to who knows what kind of field. That is the motive for writing this article. I place great hope in the efforts of our domestic rubber merchants!

Mr. Tai Yan Was a Practitioner of Promoting Domestic Goods 159

— Chou Cheng

Mr. Zhang Taiyan of Yuhang passed away at 8:00 AM on the 14th of this month at No. 50 Jin Fan Road, Suzhou. When the bad news came, everyone, whether they knew him or not, expressed their condolences. In the late Qing Dynasty, he advocated revolution and was imprisoned in the Western Prison, but he did not change his aspirations. In the early Republic, Yuan Shikai tried to win him over and hired him as an advisor, but he was not used. Later, he was imprisoned, but he enjoyed himself with poetry and wine. He could be steadfast in wealth and honor, not moved by poverty and humbleness, and not yield to power. In his later years, he lectured at Wu Men and wrote extensively. At a time when morality was declining and human desires were rampant, we were relying on this master of simple learning to develop his knowledge to save people's hearts. How could we have expected that heaven would not favor him and that this wise man would depart? The country lost a veteran, and the scholarly world lost a mentor. How could we not be sad! People only know that Mr. Zhang was a revolutionary elder and a literary giant, but they do not know that he was also a practitioner of promoting domestic goods. I followed him for a long time, so I will record his good deeds in promoting domestic goods in this publication for imitation. I got to know Mr. Zhang after 1916. At that time, Li Huangpi was in power and presented him with the horizontal plaque "Southeast Simple Learning" and returned to the south, residing in a certain neighborhood in the French Concession. His son-in-law, Tai Cangsheng, was from Jiaxing and had studied at Xiushui School. He had the friendship of being from the same hometown and school as me. He introduced me to meet Mr. Zhang. At first, I thought that a revolutionary leader who had lived abroad for a long time would wear a Western suit, but my ideal did not match the reality. Mr. Zhang wore cotton and silk short shirt and pants outside, and a spun silk long gown over that. Not only did he not have the habits of a student studying abroad, but he also resembled an old country bumpkin. At that time, I was teaching at the Nanhui Volunteer School. From then on, every week, I would go to Shanghai to listen to his teachings and benefited a lot. Seeing that none of the clothes he wore were foreign goods, I asked him the reason. He said that Zhejiang Province has always produced silk, and the cotton and silk of Yuhang are even more famous. I (Mr. Zhang referred to himself) am from Zhejiang, and my籍隸 is from Yuhang. How could I not use the products of my hometown, but instead buy imported goods, causing the loss of economic rights? He also described in detail that cotton is soft and smooth and can absorb sweat. It is suitable for making short shirts and pants in both winter and summer, and it is also durable and can be called cheap and good. Before leaving, I was given a roll of cotton and silk, and he severely criticized those who were infected with Europeanization and learned only the superficial knowledge of foreigners. Regarding clothing, food, housing, and transportation, they imitated foreign countries in every way. He said that there was a joke about a gentleman's son from the countryside who studied abroad for many years. When he returned to China, he was wearing a Western suit and leather shoes, and he was proud and complacent, like a brand new person. He criticized everything in the country as worthless. One day, his father asked him to compare foreign countries with China and asked which was better. He first said that foreign countries have clear politics and united people, so the country is rich and the people are strong, which is better than China. Then he said that foreign houses are tall and spacious, and the streets are flat, so living is comfortable, which is better than China. His father was nodding in agreement when his son suddenly pointed to the moon in the sky and said, "I don't know why the moon in foreign countries is also brighter and more lovely than the moon in China." At this time, his father realized that he was blindly following, so he spoke nonsense. The above is a joke, but in fact, there are people who hate domestic goods and love foreign goods. They regard everything in China as dung and regard foreign goods as treasures. We, who study and understand the principles, should take a firm stand and not be possessed by foreign objects, so that we can save the already collapsing situation. His words were earnest and worthy of admiration. Therefore, there were very few imported goods among all the utensils and clothes in Taiyan's family. He bought Platinum Dragon cigarettes from the Nanyang Tobacco Company. Friends and relatives knew that he was a practitioner of promoting domestic goods, so the items they sent were also limited to domestic goods. I am afraid that outsiders know very little about this matter, so I will specifically point it out to inform the readers.

Educational News

The Municipal Secondary and Normal School Graduation Joint Examination Concludes Successfully 160

Marking has begun. Results will be announced in two weeks. Regulations for students who fail to advance to higher education or serve.

The municipal joint graduation examination for secondary and normal schools for the second semester of the 24th year of the Republic of China began on the 22nd and concluded successfully yesterday. Marking has begun, and details are as follows:

Successful conclusion. Yesterday was the second day. This year's examination concluded successfully because there were fewer subjects. The situation in the examination hall was still good. All test papers are stored in the office of the Joint Examination Committee, Zeng Huji. The marking committee for each subject has also begun marking. Because there are many candidates participating in this year's examination, marking is quite time-consuming. Work is now being accelerated, and results can be announced in about two weeks.

Calculating scores. The method for calculating the scores of each subject in this year's joint examination is to take 40% of the school's graduation score for each subject and 60% of the joint examination score for each subject. The combined score will be calculated using a percentage system. Decimals below the integer will be rounded off. 80 to 100 points is Grade A, 70 to 79 points is Grade B, 60 to 69 points is Grade C, and less than 60 points is Grade D. Grades A and B are passing, and Grade D is failing.

Advancement to higher education and service. Only those who pass all subjects in the graduation joint examination can graduate. Those who fail three or more subjects will be held back. Those who cannot be held back due to special circumstances may be given a certificate of completion by the original school, stating the scores of each subject in the graduation joint examination, and stamped with the graduation joint examination failure stamp. Those who fail one or two subjects will be allowed to continue to participate in the joint examination for those subjects twice in the next two years. They can only graduate after passing. If they still fail any subjects, they should take the Ministry of Education's joint examination subjects in the future. Students who fail one or two subjects and wish to go to higher education immediately may have the Education Bureau issue a certificate to apply for higher education, with a photo of the student attached, stamped with the Education Bureau seal, and stating the scores of each subject in the graduation joint examination. They will be allowed to apply for higher education first and be admitted as probationary students. After passing the joint examination for those subjects and obtaining a graduation certificate, they will be allowed to participate in the final semester examination or graduation examination of the school they have entered. Students who fail one or two subjects and go to other provinces or cities for higher education or service may have the original school submit a request to the Education Bureau to forward it to the education administrative organ in the area where the student is studying or serving, to allow them to participate in the local graduation joint examination to make up for the examination of those subjects.

Focuses on inventions related to culture. Scheduled to open in Shanghai on October 1 this year.

The Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Cultural Construction Association is hosting the Chinese Invention Exhibition in the past ten years. After the exhibition is over, the review committee will determine the level of the inventions based on the size of their contribution to culture, and the association will give encouragement and apply for central commendation.

President Jiang's Instructions 169

Nanjing, 23rd. President Jiang summoned the athletes participating in the World Games and the members of the sports inspection team to Germany on the 23rd to give instructions. The main points of the instructions are as follows: He said that your visit to Germany to participate in the World Games is a representative of the new China. Your success or failure is related to the honor and disgrace of the country. I hope you will work hard and win glory for the motherland. Now, as you are about to leave, I would like to give you a few words of encouragement. I hope you will pay special attention to them. You should know that the central purpose of the World Games is to promote the true spirit of martial arts, that is, the spirit of "propriety, justice, integrity, and shame" advocated by the New Life Movement. Specifically, it is to respect morality, value public virtue, abide by discipline, pay attention to order, have courage and know the direction, and compete with propriety. The "sportsman's spirit" referred to in the West is to take its ability to maintain a spirit of honesty and love, abide by strict rules, and conduct peaceful and fair competitions. The meaning is also the same. Your participation in the World Games this time, the victory or defeat of the competition is not of great importance. The most important thing is to show the world the inherent spirit of propriety, justice, integrity, and shame of our country and nation. If morality is related to spiritual degeneration, then even if the competition is won, it is still a shame and a failure. If morality is not damaged and the spirit is noble, then even if the competition is lost, it is still glorious and victorious. Therefore, your participation in the World Games this time must win glory for our country in terms of moral spirit and discipline. All attitudes and actions must be based on morality, abide by regulations, be brave and know propriety, and only compete for virtue. At any time and in any place, you must show the demeanor of a dignified citizen of East Asia with a 5,000-year glorious history and a noble culture. Only then can you gain the respect and love of people from all countries in the world. I hope you will work hard and wish you health and triumph.

The delegation participating in the World Games, except for the football team that has already left the country and the cyclist who is far away in the Netherlands, took a special train to Nanjing yesterday to listen to instructions. After President Jiang personally gave the flag, they took the night train and arrived in Shanghai this morning.

All circles in this city, in view of the fact that our country's delegation will go to Germany to attend the World Games and promote national glory, have organized the Shanghai All Circles Farewell Meeting to the World Games Delegation. A joint meeting was held in the Municipal Government Auditorium and it was decided to hold a farewell ceremony at the YMCA of China in Baxianqiao at 4:00 PM today to express respect.

The National Sports Association received a letter from the Shanghai All Circles Farewell Meeting to the World Games Delegation, which stated: "Regarding the fact that your delegation is about to leave the country to participate in the World Games, all circles have specifically decided to hold a farewell meeting at the YMCA of China in Baxianqiao at 4:00 PM on June 24 to express respect. Therefore, we hereby inform you and hope that all your country's representatives and athletes will attend at that time. This is a special request. To the World Games Delegation, etc." All teams and athletes concentrated in Shanghai, as well as all members of the inspection team, are requested to attend on time to support the grand event of sports.

City Residents' Education Center Weightlifting Competition 171

Chang Guan-qun lifts 698 pounds, awards to be given at the center on July 5th

The weightlifting competition organized by the Municipal Public Education Center was held last Sunday (the 21st) in the center's Children's Life Garden. A total of 51 competitors including Chang Guan-qun participated. Ye Liang, Weng Kang-yan, and Ye Yu-shu served as referees, and the atmosphere was exceptionally lively. The details of the competition are compiled as follows:

Elimination System Adopted

The competition began at exactly 2:00 PM that afternoon. Due to the large number of participants, and the fact that this type of competition is very time-consuming, it was decided in the referees' meeting to adopt an elimination system. A reasonable standard was first determined, and only those who could meet this standard were allowed to proceed with the snatch, clean and jerk competitions. Those who could not meet the standard were immediately eliminated. Weight was then measured, and competitors were divided into five weight classes based on their weight: light, light-middle, middle, middle-heavy, and heavy.

Competition Results

Lightweight class: 1st place, Hua Feng-chun, lifted 42 pounds; 2nd place, Ding Da-xiong, Zhang San, Zhang Jin-san. Light-middleweight class: 1st place, Chen Jin-sheng, lifted 480 pounds; 2nd place, Bo Yin-sheng; 3rd place, Cheng Yu-zhen. Middleweight class: 1st place, Lu Ji-gang, lifted 516 pounds; 2nd place, Hui Bo-yu; 3rd place, Lin Chang. Light-heavyweight class: 1st place, Yu Yong-shui, lifted 552 pounds; 2nd place, Jia An-tai; 3rd place, Zhu De-sheng.

Astonishing Record

In the heavyweight class, only Chang Li-shi Guan-qun participated. His performance that day was particularly outstanding, breaking his own record of 680 pounds set in the World Games preliminaries, and setting a new record of 689 pounds.

Awards Scheduled

The center has scheduled an awards ceremony for 10:00 AM on July 5th in the center's lecture hall to provide encouragement. It is reported that a large batch of prizes from the Ge Zi Yang Hang company have already been delivered to the center, and prizes from various other organizations and companies will also be delivered soon.

Municipal No. 1 Stadium Amateur Tennis Tournament 172

Rong Qi-zhao and Li Hui-tang Discuss the Southern Expedition of the Soccer Team The Batavia Team is the Strongest 177

Our country's World Games soccer team traveled south and was invincible. When they arrived in Medan, local reporters interviewed team leader Rong Qi-zhao and captain Li Hui-tang, who provided detailed accounts of the southern expedition. Excerpts from their conversation are as follows:

Rong Qi-zhao's Account: Question: "Your team has already played over ten matches on this southern expedition. From your observation, which team would you consider the most formidable?" Answer: "The most formidable teams, with strong and skilled players, are the Singapore Armed Forces Team and the Batavia Team. However, the strength of a team can only be determined after three or four matches. It is not accurate to draw conclusions based on a single victory or defeat." Question: "Which performance by your team on this southern expedition was the best?" Answer: "From my observation, the best performance was against the Batavia All-Stars. However, our team's purpose in playing against teams in various locations is to observe the skills of others, learn from their strengths, and compensate for our own weaknesses. It is also to train our players' combat abilities and prevent their skills from deteriorating. For this reason, during the matches, we rotated players who had not played, giving each player an opportunity to compete and improve their skills, as well as the overall team coordination."

Li Hui-tang's Account: Question: "Mr. Li, you are traveling to Southeast Asia again. How do you feel about the situation of overseas Chinese in various places, compared to what you saw on your previous two trips?" Answer: "Overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia seem to be paying more attention to sports recently. During our team's southern expedition, overseas Chinese accounted for over 70% of the spectators at the matches we visited. This indicates that overseas Chinese are now emphasizing sports." Question: "From your observation, which team was the most formidable among the teams that the World Games team played against on this southern expedition?" Answer: "The Batavia Team is the strongest. However, it is difficult to assess their true strength based on just one or two matches." Question: "Which team's performance was the best among the teams the World Games team played against on this southern expedition?" Answer: "Regarding this, we dare not boast about which match was our best performance. However, our team's players have some quirks. In a match against a strong opponent, our players not only fight bravely, but also perform exceptionally well. If the opponent's strength is mediocre, our performance seems to be less energetic. In addition, the quality of the soccer field also affects our team's performance. Our team emphasizes coordination and uses a short-passing attack strategy. If the field is too hard, we sometimes find it difficult to control the bouncing ball. If the field is too soft, the ball moves slowly when passed." Question: "Which soccer field in Southeast Asia is the best?" Answer: "The Singapore field is the most suitable."

My Country's World Games Soccer Team European Travel Notes June 12th, Sent by Li Hui-tang from Medan 178

A Public Letter to Friends at Home

Time flies. It has been over a month since the soccer team stepped out of the country. We have been busy putting on our soccer boots and going out on the field, and I haven't been able to find time to report to my friends on the details of our trip. I am truly uneasy about this. If I could, I would be happy to write a long letter to each of my good friends, but there are so many good friends, and there is no way to do that.

Therefore, I would like to use the esteemed space in the newspaper to write this public letter. Although this public letter is not written for you individually, I hope that you will all treat it as a letter written specifically for you, and understand my sincere intentions. Indeed, when I write this public letter, the surprised faces of my friends are flowing in my mind, giving me infinite encouragement and joy.

When we left Shanghai and Hong Kong, we were deeply grateful to the friends who were able to come and see us off. It gave us, a group of pursuers with a vague future, a lot of comfort. The passionate emotions expressed on their faces still linger in my mind and are constantly replayed on my little screen. Since leaving the country until today, although the days have not been many, we have traveled a lot of miles. The distance traveled by ship, train, airplane, car, horse-drawn carriage, rickshaw, and on foot is quite amazing when added together. We have been to no less than twenty cities, including Saigon, Singapore, Batavia, Bandung, Surabaya, Malang, Semarang, Solo, and Medan. It is a pity that we were in a hurry and could only take a quick look, so we can't really talk about any incidents we observed. Our impressions are also very vague. The most obvious and easy to see is that the overseas Chinese have great expectations for us. This is a great comfort in the lonely journey, and it has increased our courage a lot.

Now, the battle in Southeast Asia is mostly over. After Medan, we will go to Penang and India for performances. On July 9th, we will gather with all the athletes participating in the World Games in Bombay and set off for Europe. I will talk about what happens next when I have time. At the same time, I hope my friends will not be stingy with their advice and will give me some guidance within the realm possible (please send it to Berlin).

Finally, I can reassure you all that, thanks to the efforts of the Great Alliance, we have only drawn once and have not lost in the fifteen battles we have fought so far. Just imagine that in the hot weather of Southeast Asia, with a tight schedule, unfavorable terrain, and the hardships of traveling and fighting across thousands of miles, we have been able to achieve such excellent results. Isn't that great? Below is a grand review of our achievements. I am afraid that soccer fans across the country, apart from you, will also be happy to see it first. Please do, and I wish you all progress and a happy summer! Hui-tang, June 9th, Medan

Oil Market: May Tung Oil Export Situation 179

According to the report of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, the amount of tung oil exported in May that passed inspection and was approved for export was 7,578.63 metric tons, a decrease of over 11,000 metric tons compared to the 18,583.92 metric tons in the same month last year. At first glance, it seems that tung oil exports are in a state of sharp decline. However, looking at the total amount for the first five months of this year, this year still exceeds last year by about 5,000 metric tons. This shows that the decline in export figures in May does not seem to be a sign of trade decline. In recent months, the tung oil market has been brisk and prices have been firm, which is rare in history. Although the Italo-Ethiopian War has ended and domestic and foreign tung oil prices have changed slightly, the market atmosphere is still quite stable. In addition, there is a shortage of spot goods in Shanghai and Hankou, and holders are generally holding on to their goods and expecting prices to rise, resulting in quieter transactions and a sharp reduction in export volume. As for domestic sales, the market in May was also quieter. Domestic circulation was 215.72 metric tons, compared to 317.98 metric tons at the same time last year. This year, since January, it has been 7,481.83 metric tons, compared to 5,184.45 metric tons at the same time last year (metric tons as the unit). —Exports to foreign countries—

Yarn and Cotton: Hot and Dry Weather, US Cotton Prices Rising Sharply 180

Yesterday, the US cotton market opened with brokers selling off, long positions closing, Southern hedging, and Liverpool and European sellers. Prices for various months fell by 2 to 7 points. However, prices rebounded due to buying by peers, spot traders, the Far East, New Orleans, short covering, and speculators. The weather in the Northwest region is too hot and there is a lack of rain. Before the close, some long positions closed out. Spot prices rose by 9 points, and futures prices rose by 5 to 9 points. English cotton spot prices fell by 5 points, and futures prices fell by 1 point. Indian cotton initially fell due to reports of rain, but later rose due to buying by Japanese traders and short covering. Transactions were limited.
